The Report of the Special Commissioner of the Sino-Foreign Relief Association on the Survey of the Disaster Situation in Shandong 142

The Sino-Foreign Relief Association obtained news of the Yellow River breach and immediately dispatched a special commissioner to conduct an on-site investigation to carry out relief efforts. The report of the commissioner's investigation of the disaster situation in Jining, Jiaxiang, Juye, and Dan City counties in Shandong after first inspecting the disaster situation in Henan Province is recorded below: Jining County has the largest area and the busiest streets. Considering the county's farmland, less than three-tenths of it was flooded. After passing the Shunxiang River Road, the water is still one or two feet deep. Nearby farmland, yellow beans, and late wheat are all submerged and unharvested. The Xintao River, 20 miles outside the South Gate, was flooded by about 200 hectares. In the seventh district, there is a vast expanse of water, and the water has not receded to two or three feet. There are too many village names to record in detail. Jiaxiang County has the smallest area, but there are many mountains and plains. Two-thirds of the autumn crops planted were flooded. In Dongguan Township, 600 mu of farmland were completely flooded, and more than 1,000 households were affected. 5,000 disaster victims are awaiting relief, and no one has provided relief yet. Juye County has a slightly larger area than Jiaxiang, and one-third of the autumn grain planted was submerged. After passing the Pig Water River, it was witnessed that the inside of the embankments on both sides was still a vast expanse of water. (Dan City County) has an even larger area than Juye. The water marks in various places are as deep as six feet, and the water has not receded to six or seven inches. There is no harvest. The disaster situation in the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts is the most serious. It is reported that the association is extremely broad and has a large population of disaster victims. The weather is already cold, and cotton clothing and winter work all need to be prepared. The relief is very difficult. There is an urgent need for all sectors to assist so that it can proceed as soon as possible.

The Military and Political Department Shanghai Factory Custody Office Established Yesterday 143

The Ordnance Factory Office was ordered to be abolished yesterday, and a custody office was established to manage everything within the factory. At the same time, the Processing Committee established by the Ordnance Department was also ordered by the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs to be abolished. The details of each matter are recorded as follows:

Ordered to Establish: Since the suspension of the Ordnance Factory, the Shanghai Ordnance Factory Processing Committee was established within the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs, and a Shanghai-based office was established to handle all closing matters. Although the affairs handled by the office had gradually been completed by the summer of this year, the office's title was not abolished. It was not until the day before yesterday that the factory's Processing Committee received instructions from the Ministry to abolish it and establish a Shanghai Factory Clearing Office to handle all clearing matters. At the same time, the Shanghai-based office was also abolished, and the Military and Political Department Ordnance Department Shanghai Factory Custody Office was established.

Selection of Director: After receiving the order, the Shanghai-based office immediately followed instructions to close the office and abolish its title. At the same time, the Military and Political Department Ordnance Department appointed Mr. Li Chengxu, the former director of the factory's pharmaceutical plant, as the director of the custody office, and also appointed eleven custodians to manage the objects in various sections. The office was established in the original Gaochang Temple Ordnance Factory, and yesterday began operating according to the new organization.

All Staff: According to custodian Yan Xianguang, who spoke to a reporter from the Huadong News Agency yesterday, the eleven custodians have now been assigned by Director Li to manage various sections, including military equipment (Kang Wangfeng Han), material warehouse (Wang Qiliang, Huang Rongchang), and documents (assigned to Yu). Other custodians are responsible for the custody of the Gaochang Temple Shell Factory, Artillery Factory, Machine Factory, Gun Factory, and Longhua Pharmaceutical Factory. The custody office has a company of guards left over from the former Ordnance Factory, with a platoon as a detachment, which is still responsible for guard duties.

Reefs Discovered on the Southeast Coast 144

Navigators must pay attention

The Hydrographic Survey Bureau of the Navy Department recently surveyed the sea lanes on the southeast coast and discovered reefs northeast of Dapeng Cape in Dapeng Bay. Its position is at 180.5 degrees north from the summit of Chiyang Mountain (2810 feet high), a distance of 2.95 nautical miles, that is, approximately 114 degrees 33 minutes east longitude and 22 degrees 29 minutes north latitude. Its current state is only 2 feet above the water surface. This place is an important shipping route, and navigators must pay attention.

Existing Companies Should Complete Re-registration 151

The Social Affairs Bureau issued an instruction to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday stating: "To comply with the order, we received instruction No. 19541 from the Ministry of Industry stating that existing companies that have not been registered should uniformly apply for registration in accordance with the law before September 30 of this year. This has already been ordered and filed. Now, according to a report from the Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, based on a report from the Beijing Municipal Federation of Factories, for the re-registration of existing companies, how should the legally required documents, such as the inspection certificate from the competent authority, the investigation report from directors, supervisors, and committee members, and the resolution record of the establishment meeting, be supplemented? We propose to specially order a method to be forwarded to the Ministry for review and instructions. After investigating that existing companies have all been established for many years, and were not handled in accordance with the Company Law at the time of their original establishment, the currently prepared registration documents cannot be in accordance with the law. Now, in order to comply with the facts and the law, we have specially ordered four articles of methods for supplementing the registration documents of existing companies, and a copy is enclosed for your compliance and forwarding to all company members for their information. This order includes the following methods: (1) If the shares of an existing company are fully subscribed by the promoters, they should supplement the request to the competent authority for inspection in accordance with the law and issue an inspection certificate. (2) If the shares of an existing company are not fully subscribed by the promoters, the current directors and supervisors should conduct a re-investigation and issue a report, requesting the shareholders' meeting to approve it. (3) The resolution record of the establishment meeting can be replaced by the resolution record of the shareholders' meeting that recently amended the articles of association, the resolution record of the shareholders' meeting that elected the current directors and supervisors, and the resolution record of the shareholders' meeting that approved the investigation report of the directors and supervisors in the preceding article. (4) In order to complete the procedures in the first and second articles, if an existing company cannot supplement the request for registration within the time limit, it may state the reasons within the time limit and formally apply for registration after the time limit, but the time must be declared in advance and approved by the Ministry of Industry."

Jisheng Association Specializes in Urgent Relief for the Sisha Flood Disaster 157

According to reports from the China Jisheng Association, the four sands of Shidong, Zhongxin, Changxing, and Dingfeng, across from the town of Wusong in Baoshan County, were suddenly hit by a hurricane and heavy rain on September 2 of this year. The tide surged, collapsing more than 500 houses, and about 600 people and livestock were washed away and drowned. More than 3,000 disaster victims are awaiting rescue. The disaster situation is unprecedented. The association purchased 160 shi of relief rice and sent personnel to the disaster area to distribute it according to the severity of the disaster, all by personally visiting the homes of the disaster victims on a temporary basis. Regardless of the size of the household, it was distributed in three grades, totaling 9.6 he, 4.8 he, and 4 qian per person. A total of 28 shi 2 dou 2 sheng 4 he of relief rice was distributed in Shidong Sand, 20 shi 0 sheng 4 he in Zhongxin Sand, 91 shi 9 dou 2 sheng in Changxing Sand, and 20 shi 0 sheng 4 he in Dingfeng Sand, totaling 160 shi of relief rice. There were also 5 dou 8 sheng 4 he of leftover rice, which were also distributed together. Although the disaster victims were slightly relieved, they were hit by hurricanes and torrential rains again the day before yesterday, and the disaster situation in various places is even worse. How can we have the magic touch to save these millions of compatriots waiting to die?

Tobacco and Alcohol Industries Request Amendment of New Regulations, Ministry Rejects 158

The Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industries Joint Association had previously submitted opinions on the obstacles in the new regulations on local tobacco and alcohol taxes, requesting the Ministry of Finance to amend them. Yesterday, they received a reply from the Ministry of Finance stating: "The summary and memorandum have been noted. After careful review of the memorandum and the documents submitted by the Taxation Department regarding the association's repeated submissions and telegrams, regarding the new regulations on local tobacco and alcohol, either due to misinterpretation of the provisions, causing misunderstandings, or advocating the maintenance of bad habits, being used by others. For example, the new regulations set fixed-amount taxes and measure-based rates, each with a fixed procedure, so that merchants know the exact amount they should pay, and officials have no way to collect excessive or harsh taxes, which was originally intended to protect the interests of merchants and people, but the merchants hold different opinions and make accusations. What is their intention? It should be known that the commercial monopolies that have been maintained over the years, with layer upon layer of corruption, have been criticized by the world. The Minister is determined to eliminate this in order to alleviate the people's difficulties. However, the summary still considers the old system to be convenient, as if deeply regretting its abolition. Why are the likes and dislikes so different? Also, there is much haggling over the penalties. I don't know that the penalties are specifically for those who conceal or omit. If the merchants are engaged in legitimate business and ask themselves if they have no other intentions, why worry about being strict? The containers for local alcohol are too complicated. If the alcohol merchants can set uniform standards themselves, the standards can be assessed according to the containers. As for the meaning of unified taxation, the association's submission is not yet fully understood. Unified taxation means that one tax is levied on one item and no re-taxation is levied, which has nothing to do with whether there is a factory or not. The fixed-amount tax on local alcohol this time is based on provinces, which is different from the nature of unified taxation. Whether to change to unified taxation in the future or set other methods is something that the Ministry will consider on its own. There is no need for the association to plan in advance. As for the selection of bureau personnel, the Ministry has always taken the principle of using people according to their talents. If there are those who do not abide by the regulations and take the opportunity to extort, those merchants can first file a factual complaint with the provincial bureau, and there is also the Taxation Department and the Ministry to which they can appeal, and it is not difficult to deal with them impartially. There is no need to worry too much. Moreover, the reform of the tax system has just been established and the regulations have not yet been announced. If there are any objections, and the association is established at this time, as if it has a preconceived opinion, the Minister has reviewed the entire file. The Taxation Department has already reviewed and replied separately to the reasons and requests for improvement submitted directly by the various industry associations, such as the commutation of methods for supplementary tax payment for inventory and tax refunds, the order of local alcohol tax payment, the length of the transportation and change of transportation periods, the procedures for calculating taxes on foreign cigarettes, and the regulations for various tax refunds on local tobacco. The merchants of each industry should be able to understand this and implement it conscientiously. If, after operating in accordance with the new regulations, difficulties are found in the procedures after a considerable period of time, those merchants can submit the facts to the Taxation Department for review and handling, provided that they do not conflict with the principles. However, they must not make empty demands, nor should they use the cessation of brewing and transportation as a tool for obstruction and sabotage, as submitted in the summary. If they dare to violate this, they will be dealt with strictly in accordance with the law to emphasize tax administration. Do not say that you were not warned. This reply."

Rescuing the Sale of Chinese Tea to Russia 160

Shanghai Banking Circles Have Difficulty Lending, Chinese-Russian Tea Merchants Begin Trading

Tea is a major export of our country. However, in recent years, due to adhering to outdated methods and poor roasting, it has been affected by the dumping of Indian, Ceylonese, and Japanese tea. Chinese tea has plummeted in the international market. Tea merchants have suffered heavy losses due to excessive stockpiling. The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry convened meetings of various tea merchants to discuss, and agreed on rescue and improvement methods, and submitted them to the Ministry of Industry for adoption and implementation. The annual amount of Chinese tea sold to Russia is quite large. However, Russian merchants have traditionally not traded in cash when purchasing Chinese tea, and it takes a year before the money is paid in full. However, Chinese tea merchants have been unable to lend money due to poor business and economic difficulties in recent years, so the sale of Chinese tea to Russia has been suspended in an invisible way. Various export tea merchants have submitted requests to the International Trade Bureau to forward them to the Ministry of Industry for assistance. After further consultation between the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance, it was decided that the Ministries of Finance and Industry, together with the tea merchants, would contact the banking circles in Shanghai to negotiate loan methods. A reporter from New News Agency learned from the Trade Bureau yesterday that this matter has been properly discussed by the Ministries of Finance and Industry, tea merchants, and banking circles in Shanghai, and the methods have been decided, as follows: (1) After the tea trade between China and Russia is concluded, Russian merchants will be allowed one year to repay the money, and the money will be advanced by the banking circles. (2) After one year, the Russian merchants will repay the principal and interest in full to the bank that advanced the money. The above two methods have already been agreed upon by the banking circles. The Shanghai Russian Merchants Association has already started handling the shipment of goods for sale in Russia.

Our Country's Rice and Wheat Markets 162

Are Almost Completely Manipulated by Foreign Goods, Large Quantities Imported Annually, Various Parties Request Import Tariffs

Our country is an agricultural country, and the rice and wheat produced in various provinces are sufficient to be self-sufficient and have a surplus. However, in recent years, the rural economy of the whole country has gone bankrupt. The reason for this is that although it is caused by frequent natural disasters and man-made disasters in successive years, the dumping of foreign rice and foreign wheat is the main reason. The chairmen of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Henan provinces, as well as the National General Chamber of Commerce, have successively telegraphed the government, requesting the imposition of import tariffs on foreign rice in order to save the sales of domestic grain and restore the rural economy. The Ministry of Finance is now carefully considering this matter, and concrete measures will be decided soon. The reporter from New News Agency believed that this matter is related to the entire economic problem of our country, so he went to the International Trade Bureau and the Jianghai Customs to investigate the dumping of foreign rice and wheat and the quantities, as well as the detailed impact on our country. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Foreign Rice Floods the Market 163

Our country's rice production can originally be self-sufficient. If there is a bumper harvest, there is still a surplus. However, in recent years, due to the dumping of foreign rice, the sales of Chinese rice have been sluggish. This year's autumn harvest is abundant, but foreign rice is still continuously imported and floods the market, selling at low prices. The quantity of imports has increased sharply year by year. Last year's imports were 22,486,639 dan, a sharp increase of more than double compared to the previous year's 10,740,810 dan, with a value of 100 million gold units. Although there are no statistics for this year yet, the import quantity will still exceed last year's statistics. Domestic rice merchants have suffered heavy losses due to stockpiling. Although the disaster situation in various places is widespread this year, rice production has not been severely affected, so the harvests are very abundant. If foreign rice is allowed to be imported and dumped continuously, it will directly threaten our country's rice market, and indirectly affect the bankruptcy of the rural economy.

Foreign Wheat Dumping 164

Our country's wheat has also been declining sharply in recent years. The reason for this is not that domestic wheat production is too abundant, but that most factories in our country use foreign wheat, and foreign goods are all surplus products from their own countries, dumped in our country, with prices falling sharply. Chinese wheat has also declined accordingly, so the wheat market is completely manipulated by foreign wheat. This year's domestic wheat production is also very abundant, but surplus wheat from foreign countries is still imported continuously, causing wheat in various parts of our country to be stockpiled and unsalable.

Rice and Wheat Statistics 165

According to the Jianghai Customs survey, the statistics of foreign wheat imports last year are as follows: A. Foreign rice imports: (1) More than 7.5 million dan from Annam, worth more than 34 million gold units; (2) More than 7.16 million dan from British India, worth more than 30.8 million gold units; (3) More than 6.4 million dan from Siam, worth more than 29 million gold units; (4) More than 1.1 million dan from Hong Kong, worth more than 5.5 million gold units; (5) A total of more than 22.4 million dan from other countries, worth more than 100 million gold units. B. Wheat imports: (1) More than 9.2 million dan from Australia, worth 30 million gold units; (2) More than 2.9 million dan from the United States, worth 7 million gold units; (3) More than 2.7 million dan from Canada, worth 7 million gold units; (4) A total of more than 15 million dan from other countries, worth more than 43 million gold units.

Freight Train Service Between Shanghai and Beiping Suspended Before Capital Ferry Opens 175

Due to low freight volume and uneconomical operation, the Transportation Department is authorized to handle ferry crossing fees, which will be collected in cash.

After the implementation of the joint transportation train service between Shanghai and Beiping on September 1, the Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Administrations stipulated that trains No. 401 and No. 402 on the Jinghu Line would be used for joint transportation of goods between Shanghai and Beiping, and strictly prohibited staff from bringing relatives and friends on the Shanghai-Beiping train. The Ministry's regulations stipulate military transportation and government accounting methods, which are detailed below.

Operation of Freight Trains 176

The railway recently revised its train schedule, stipulating that trains No. 401 and No. 402 on the Jinghu Line are specifically for loading goods for joint transportation between Shanghai and Beiping. Before the ferry is completed, trains will depart daily from both Jinghu stations once each for upstream and downstream operations. However, because vehicles cannot currently cross the river directly, the amount of goods loaded is extremely limited. Moreover, the departure times of these trains are earlier than other trains, so they often cannot catch up even when used to load goods from this line. As a result, a train departs on schedule, but carries very few goods, wasting the capacity of the locomotive and vehicles, which is uneconomical. The authority to operate these two trains will be temporarily delegated to the Transportation Department to carefully handle the freight situation along the line before the ferry is completed, in order to avoid waste. A report will be submitted to the Ministry of Railways for record.

Strict Prohibition of Staff Riding the Train 177

The opening of the Jinghu Line's 301 and 302 Shanghai-Beiping joint transportation trains is extremely important for railway revenue. All fares must be collected in cash. All discounted accounting, or free preferential certificates, half-price military tickets, half-price tickets for various National Government departments, and accounting trailers are not applicable. The Vehicle Department has forwarded the Ministry's order to all departments for compliance. In order to strictly enforce the decree, the department yesterday sent another letter to all relevant personnel, stating that (except for employees who are actually serving on the train, other people holding any official travel permits or service travel licenses are not applicable and must purchase tickets separately to ride the train. If any train staff members allow relatives and friends to ride the train without tickets, or collude and allow them to ride with inapplicable tickets, they will be dismissed immediately upon verification, without leniency.

Ferry Fees Collected in Cash 178

After the opening of the capital ferry, the methods for military transportation and government accounting transportation have been approved by the Executive Yuan after being submitted by the Ministry of Railways as follows: (1) All ferry crossing fees will be collected in cash and will not be accounted for. (2) Shanghai-Beiping joint transportation direct special express trains, Shanghai-Beiping-Hutong joint transportation direct freight trains, and segmented responsible joint transportation direct freight trains, whether upstream or downstream, are not applicable to government accounting or discount methods, and military transportation with accounting or discounts. (3) Other trains on each line, such as those with chapter regulations, and special restrictions, will be handled according to past methods, except that ferry crossing fees will be collected in cash. (4) Regarding military, military supplies, and military equipment, ammunition, and other vehicles, they should be allowed to cross the ferry, but they must comply with the following requirements: A. All ferry crossing fees will be collected in cash. B. Comply with the Capital Railway Ferry Joint Transportation Freight Vehicle Inspection Regulations promulgated by the Ministry. Special attention should be paid to the restrictions in Article 3 (A) to (E) of the regulations. C. Although these vehicles are allowed to cross the ferry, this transportation has always been the responsibility of the originating agency to send personnel to escort them, and should still be handled according to previous regulations. The railway cannot be responsible. D. Due to the gradient on both sides of the ferry crossing, it is easy to cause danger. The loading of the interior of these vehicles should be given special attention by the originating agency, and should be carefully handled under the guidance of railway personnel. Also, explosives such as dynamite, gunpowder, bombs, hand grenades, etc., which the railway deems dangerous and unsuitable for crossing the ferry, shall not be allowed to cross the ferry to ensure safety. E. In addition to carrying Shanghai-Beiping joint transportation direct express train passenger cars across the river, the ferry should give priority to carrying ordinary freight trains across the river. It has been found that the construction of the capital ferry was funded by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity, and principal and interest must be repaid monthly in the future, and it is also the second guarantee for the Yuehan Railway loan. This has been clearly stated in case No. 417 of the complete collection of full fees for Shanghai-Beiping traffic, and has been approved. Therefore, no matter what type of vehicle crosses the river, it is necessary to collect the ferry crossing fee in cash. In addition, the ferry's capacity to transport vehicles is limited, so it is necessary to slightly restrict it to maintain traffic and emphasize railway administration. In order to avoid future disputes and misunderstandings, the above regulations must be formulated in fact, in order to achieve the effect of careful beginnings and uniformity.

Du Chongyuan's Speech on September 18th 181

Du Chongyuan, President of the China National Products Cooperative, gave a special speech on the National Humiliation of September 18th at the Sichuan Road YMCA. Ms. Liang, a stenographer from the Bingxun Stenography Agency, recorded the speech. Although it was raining heavily that day, many people attended the meeting. The following is an excerpt from his speech: "The Chinese people think that the September 18th Incident was something that came out of the blue. However, this national disaster did not happen overnight. Since Japan destroyed Korea, it has had the ambition to invade our Northeast. Since the Russo-Japanese War, it has tried its best to control all undertakings in the Northeast, preparing to occupy our Northeast. After the Meiji Restoration, it actively instilled the idea of invading China into its own people, and tried its best to prevent our national movement, sometimes using economic power and sometimes using political power. These are all steps in its progress towards China. It tried its best to show China's shortcomings and all kinds of bad things, and taught its own people to admire the strengths of the British and American countries and not to learn China's shortcomings. But on the one hand, it tried its best to hide the rich resources of China's land and instill them into the minds of its ordinary people. The methods it used were entirely commercialized. The biscuits it ate were printed with the names of our three northeastern provinces: Jilin, Fengtian, and Heilongjiang. When customers came to buy them, they didn't ask to buy biscuits, but to buy Jilin, Fengtian, or Heilongjiang. When they met those small customers, they even asked them one by one if they liked them. If they said they liked them, they would say to them, 'These are fake Jilin, Fengtian, and Heilongjiang. If they were real Jilin, Fengtian, and Heilongjiang, they would be hundreds of times better!' There was also a kind of biscuit called 'Manzhou.' All of these were actions aimed at annexing the Northeast. In the political sphere, it often sent large groups of workers to work in our Northeast, while at the same time investigating the situation in the Northeast. Almost all Japanese people in the Northeast had a map of Manzhou. What the people it had in the Northeast did was nothing more than work to invade and occupy Manzhou. For example, if it ran a newspaper, it would use the power of the news to cater to the psychology of our people and win them over. For example, when warlords like Zhang Zongchang and Zhang Zuolin were rampant, they would say in the newspapers how those warlords were harming the people, while at the same time showing how much their own government loved the people. These were all facts before September 18th. It took active actions everywhere, but what about us? We almost always failed. Only the 19th Route Army and the Northeast Volunteer Army won a few victories, but the result was still failure. We must have a unified direction and unite in order to save our China. Therefore, talking about the national humiliation of September 18th is nothing more than wanting everyone to unite together. If we can unite together and resist with one heart and one mind, then China will have a day of revival."

Comparison of Speed of Mail to Europe 182

The Shanghai Times reported that yesterday (19th) it was said that mail from Europe to Shanghai, if labeled with the words "via Siberia and Dalian," could arrive in Shanghai earlier. The local postal authorities have denied this. It is said that labeling mail with the word "Dalian" is not enough to affect the delivery route of the mail. Unless the postal authorities of the countries concerned have separately agreed on a special agreement, it will still be delivered according to the usual route. As for mail from Europe to Shanghai via Siberia, the route it takes to Shanghai after arriving at the Siberian border is entirely determined by the Soviet authorities. At present, mail from Europe to Shanghai via Siberia often takes a month to arrive, while mail sent to Hong Kong via the same route only takes 20 to 22 days. This is because one route is via Vladivostok and Japan to Shanghai, while the other route is via Dalian to Hong Kong.

Truth Revealed in the Case of the Tobacco and Paper Shop Clerk Being Falsely Accused of Theft 183

Luo Jishang Acquitted and Released

Wang Wengen, a clerk at the Dongchang Tobacco and Paper Shop on Wusong Road, was carrying 1,300 yuan in cash on June 5th when he was suddenly stopped and robbed of the money by three robbers on North Suzhou Road, who then fled. Wu Leshan, one of the robbers, was subsequently captured and sent to the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, where he was interrogated and sentenced to seven years in prison. Later, the Central Police Department arrested Luo Ayin, an accomplice. After investigation, Luo suddenly falsely accused Luo Jishang, a Ningbo native who worked as a clerk at the tobacco and paper shop, of being an accomplice in the robbery, and Luo Jishang was also arrested. His relatives and friends in Shanghai immediately hired lawyer Lin Yangqing to defend him, saying that Luo Jishang had been working for several years and had always been honest, and that Luo Jiyin did not know him at all, let alone participate in the robbery. This time, he was falsely accused in an attempt to frame him. They begged for a clear investigation, a quick release, and the protection of the innocent and the importance of people's lives. After repeated summons and investigations of the case by Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the First Special Court, Huang Baochang, the manager of Qinchang, also testified that Luo Jishang did not know that Wang Wengen had been ordered to take the money out that day. Judge Qian, having learned the truth, announced his judgment yesterday: Luo Jishang was innocent, and Luo Ayin was sentenced to seven years in prison. The police representative stated that they were abandoning the appeal regarding Luo Jishang, and the court immediately released him. Luo Ayin was sent to prison.

Ship Dweller Drowns in Hurricane 184

Zhang Bing-sheng, a sampan boat dweller of the Wayside Wharf Barge Company, age 39, a native of Wusong, was moored at the Guangxing Road pier in Yangshupu on the evening of the 18th of this month. Unexpectedly, that day was marked by a severe hurricane and heavy rain in Shanghai, which snapped his mooring ropes. Zhang was unable to control the boat, leading to the capsizing of both boat and man, and they drifted away without a trace. It wasn't until 8 o'clock yesterday morning that the Customs water police, having received many reports of boat dwellers lost in the severe storm, dispatched patrol boats to investigate. They discovered the body in the Yangshupu river mouth and transported it to the South Wharf Life Saving Bureau. Detective Xu Jue-lu was also dispatched to report the finding to the local court for verification.

Huang Senquan Dies by Poisoning – Suicide Due to Wife's Elopement 185

Ding Hai-shan, a night watchman from the second division of the sixth district in Shanghai West, was patrolling Haig Road at approximately 10 o'clock last night when a passerby reported that a student was lying unconscious by the roadside on Qiaodun Road (behind Jiaotong University). Officer Ding immediately went to investigate and determined that the individual had likely ingested poison. When questioned, the student was unable to speak. Consequently, arrangements were made to transport him to the Haig Road Red Cross Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of the poisoning, rescue was impossible. He passed away at the hospital at 4 o'clock this morning. Six suicide notes were found on the deceased, signed Huang Senquan. The letters, in essence, addressed his wife, stating that the wedding expenses, totaling over a thousand yuan, were borrowed from various sources and remain unpaid. Now that she had abandoned him and pursued a new romance, he could no longer bear to live in this world and therefore resolved to commit suicide. However, no address was provided. The deceased appeared to be around 30 years old, wearing a twill student uniform, a white undershirt, reddish-gray Western socks, and had a shaved head with short hair. No other belongings were found. Yesterday afternoon, the second division of the sixth district notified the local court, which dispatched a prosecutor to conduct an examination. The examination confirmed that Huang Senquan had indeed died from poisoning. After investigating the family, instructions were given to take photos for record and to hand over the body to the local guardian for burial.

Laborer Dies After Falling from Cargo Truck 186

Yesterday morning at approximately 10 o'clock, the Shuntai Flower Clothing Store in Xinjing Town, Shanghai Northwest, hired truck number 16541 from the Fuxing Automobile Company's concession area to transport 54 bales of cotton to Shanghai. The driver, Wei Shi-liang from Changzhou, was driving when, upon turning at the intersection of Lincoln Road and Da Xi Road, the uneven road surface caused three workers sitting on top of the cotton bales - Zhang Yun-shan, Gong Bao-yuan, and Cai A-san - to fall off the truck. They sustained head injuries and severe trauma. The driver transported the three injured individuals to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, Cai A-san's injuries were too severe, and he died upon arrival at the hospital.

Impoverished Man Dies from Electrocution 187

Yesterday morning, in Baoren Alley, across from the City God Temple in the city, a poorly dressed young man, appearing to be a garbage collector, around 20 years old, accidentally touched a live wire and died instantly. Someone called the police on duty, who reported the incident to the second division of the first district. The local guardian was instructed to report the case to the local court to send someone to conduct an examination. As there were no relatives of the deceased, the charity was instructed to collect and bury the body.

Expanded National Student Anti-Drug Essay Competition 188

The Anti-Drug Association Announces Competition Guidelines

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association has decided to expand this year's anti-drug essay competition and is actively preparing for it. The majority of the preparations are already underway, and the new regulations for this year's essay competition have also been finalized. They are hereby announced as follows: (1) Purpose: To encourage students in universities and middle schools to study the opium problem and participate in the anti-drug movement. (2) Registration: Registration must be done using the designated registration form, signed and stamped by the school principal as proof, and sent to the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association at No. 19 Bowuyuan Road, Shanghai. Each school is limited to two participants. The registration deadline is November 15, 1933. (3) Manuscripts: Manuscripts can be written in either modern or classical Chinese. Each entry should not exceed 6,000 characters for university students and 4,000 characters for middle school students. A list of references should be attached, signed and stamped by the principal as proof, and sent to the association by registered mail along with a photo and resume of the student. The submission deadline is December 15, 1933. (4) Topics: (A) University Division: "The Actual Situation of the Opium Plague in Our Region and Effective Eradication Plans." (Note: This topic emphasizes investigative writing. Accurate records should be kept of all issues such as the production, sale, taxation, transportation, and consumption of opium, as well as the impact of opium on society, economy, morality, and law. Everything must be based on facts and should not be empty or imaginary.) (B) Middle School Division: "The Fate of Opium Addicts." (Note: This topic emphasizes realistic fiction writing. A detailed and vivid description of the addict's life, family, reasons for addiction, and the various adverse consequences suffered after addiction is required. Do not fabricate stories out of thin air, as this will contradict the purpose of realism.) (5) Judging: The judging criteria will be based on the following points, with scores awarded separately: (A) Accuracy of factual investigation (40%), (B) Thoroughness of thought and structure (30%), (C) Clarity and conciseness of writing (30%). Judges will be academics invited by the association, and the list will be announced later. (6) Awards: Ten awards will be given in the university division and thirty awards in the middle school division. (7) Prizes: In addition to medals, certificates and monetary awards, the first, second, and third-place winners in the university division and the first, second, third, fourth, and fifth-place winners in the middle school division will receive additional scholarship funds. The distribution of prize money will be based on the amount of prize money collected and will be announced later.

Jiang Chen Sues Jiang Fuyin for Fraudulent Marriage, Abuse, and Abandonment 189

Jiang Chen, a young woman from Huaicheng, Jiangbei, residing at No. 46, 40 Jian, Rue du Père Robert in the French Concession, aged 27, has recently engaged lawyer Zhu Dianqing to file a criminal lawsuit in the Second Special Court against Jiang Fuyin, a fellow villager, for fraudulent marriage, abuse, and abandonment, seeking investigation and prosecution, with an attached civil suit. The basis of her lawsuit states that the plaintiff followed her father to Shanghai to make a living from a young age. When she reached marriageable age, the defendant, seeing that the plaintiff had some beauty and learning that her parents had some savings, became covetous. Day and night, he made various advances, and then enlisted a neighbor to act as a matchmaker to the plaintiff's mother, wanting to marry the plaintiff. The plaintiff's mother knew that he was a wolf in sheep's clothing, and instructed the plaintiff to be careful to prevent accidents. However, the defendant schemed and spoke jokingly, saying that he was single and willing to make a lifelong commitment. He also said that if she married someone else, he would kill her spouse, and if she left Shanghai, he would blind her and cut off her tendons. Before long, his attitude changed, and he was pleasant and comforting. At the time, the plaintiff ignored him, but the defendant thought that he could deceive a woman, and followed her everywhere, wanting to rape her. Unfortunately, the plaintiff's awareness was weak, and she was raped. The defendant then said that the formalities of marriage had been completed, making people believe that they were husband and wife, and found a house to live together, living in peace. However, the plaintiff's mother had no sons, so she loved her daughter like a pearl, privately hoping that she would have someone to rely on in her old age. The defendant, seeing that this first goal had been achieved, began to plot for money, borrowing repeatedly. So the plaintiff's mother lent him all her savings and membership fees, totaling more than 600 yuan. He first bought more than ten rickshaws, and several years later, he gradually accumulated funds and bought 29 rickshaws. From then on, the family was well-off, but the defendant then had the intention of abandonment, scolding and abusing her all day long, ignoring her livelihood, for half a year. She recently learned that the defendant's wife was still alive and had children. After the plaintiff married the defendant, she also had a son and a daughter. Now, he suddenly abandoned her, leaving her with no means of support. Therefore, she was forced to file a lawsuit, requesting that he be investigated and dealt with according to Article 244 of the Criminal Law, and also attached a civil suit, requesting a judgment ordering him to pay living expenses to support her. According to the complaint, the court summoned him yesterday afternoon. First, the defendant's lawyer claimed that the plaintiff had already filed a lawsuit in the local court, which was being heard today, and the defendant was being held in custody. According to the litigation regulations, one case cannot have two lawsuits, so the case should be dismissed. The plaintiff's lawyer claimed that the case was filed in this court first, but the defendant fled to the Chinese area, so she also filed a lawsuit in the local court. Whether this case should be accepted should be decided by the court. Judge Zhang Chaozuo reviewed the words and ordered it to be withdrawn and await a ruling.

Chang Chong Trading Company Convicted of Fraudulently Recruiting Workers and Collecting Money 190

Zhou Jincai from Yangzhou, from April to August of this year, impersonated the American-owned Lange Foreign Company, using the pretext of recruiting workers to haul timber in the South Seas Islands, with a monthly wage of 65 yuan. With the Turkish national Iman Mateng as manager and Zhou himself as foreman, they privately set up a recruitment agency at No. 18 Songpan Lane, Songpan Road, employing assistants such as Zhou Lichun and Zhou Jinsai. More than a hundred people were swindled, totaling more than 700 yuan. After the incident, Chinese Detective Liu Wenzao arrested Zhou and ten others and sent them to the First Special District Local Court. After repeated hearings and deliberations, the case was finally concluded and a date was set for sentencing. It was reported in detail in the newspaper. Yesterday morning, the sentencing date arrived. Judge Liu Yugui presided over the sentencing in the Third Criminal Court. Defendant Zhou Jincai was sentenced to one year in prison, Zhou Jinbao, Fei Zhaofeng, Xu Hechun, Lü Zhenmao, and Wei Fu were each sentenced to three months in prison, and Zhou Lichun was sentenced to two months in prison. The number of days of detention before the final judgment was allowed to be offset at a rate of two days for one day. The evidence was confiscated. Zhou Yushan, Wang Deyuan, Du Honglong, and Zhou Lisen were all acquitted. The police stated that they would abandon the appeal, and they were released in court.

Yesterday afternoon at 6:15, the roof of a paint shop at No. 285 Zhoujiazui Road suddenly collapsed due to years of disrepair. Fortunately, no one was injured. The fire brigade and the police went to investigate and held the owner of the house responsible.

Fresh Meat Industry Finalizes Aviation Donation 193

Decided to Allocate 100,000 Yuan – Requests Shanghai Finance Bureau to Allocate Accordingly

The aviation salvation donation undertaken by the fresh meat industry in this city was originally planned in March of this year, with the Fresh Meat Industry Association pledging to raise 100,000 yuan. However, due to internal disputes within the association, the sales industry began collecting 2 cents per pig on July 1st, but the aviation salvation donation has not yet been collected. Nevertheless, the association will find a way to collect the donation. Recently, the association sent a letter to the Aviation Association stating that after the association pledged 100,000 yuan for the aviation salvation fund, it could have started collecting in May. However, due to opposition and sabotage by a small number of colleagues, it has been delayed until now. Now, in order to save the country, the association will allocate 100,000 yuan from the public funds of the slaughter tax of 9 cents per pig, managed by the Committee for the Improvement of Slaughtering Expenses for the Inland Industry. The method is to hand over the funds and all accounting documents managed by the committee to your association and request that the committee cease its work. It is estimated that the number of pigs slaughtered annually in the inland industry is approximately 400,000, and the slaughter tax is 9 cents per pig, totaling approximately 40,000 yuan per year. Since the establishment of the committee in August 1931, the funds that it has managed, in addition to subsidies for education expenses for the children of colleagues and expenses for the North and South City Night Schools and hygiene, have not been announced, and the association has no way of knowing. After receiving the funds, your association should investigate the existing funds and allocate them to the aviation donation first. After collecting the full amount of 100,000 yuan, it should be handed back to the association for its own management. However, during the period of collection by your association, 30% of the total annual amount will still be allocated for the inland industry's hygiene improvement expenses, and 600 yuan per month will still be subsidized for the North and South City Night Schools. After receiving the letter, the Aviation Association held a meeting yesterday with representatives from all parties in the fresh meat industry. The attendees included Zhou Chengxiang, Wang Fusheng (Xujiahui), Zhang Fugen, Xu Wenhua, Yang Qiusheng (Tanzhiwan), Hu Yongchun (Pudong Laobaidu), He Chengjun (Caohejing), Qin Zucha, Chen Zhaoan, Cao Yunsong (Zhenru), Sun Huangzong, Mao Bin (Hongzhen), Wu Linfa (Qiujiang Bridge), Zhou Yueliang, Qin Yangen, Zhang Jisheng (Caojiadu), Jin Guifu, Shen Xie, Rong Qianchu, Zhu Yunxing, Ye Shifan, Ye Hengxian, Huang Jicun, Ye Dajia, Lu Jichen (Zhabei), and Zhu Zhigao (Nanshi), totaling 26 people. Li Dachao chaired the meeting, and Zhang Yuliang took notes. The chairman reported that the government is paying close attention to aviation and preparing to complete a powerful air force in the shortest possible time. The citizens of this city have suffered greatly from airplanes and know the importance of aviation. Therefore, they have taken the lead in advocating aviation salvation, enthusiastically joining the Aviation Association, and donating aviation funds. In particular, colleagues in the fresh meat industry can take on a fighter plane, and the mayor is very gratified. Rong Qianchu then reported on the donation and the process of the proposal. Mao Bin reported on the use and distribution of the 9-cent slaughter tax. Finally, all the representatives expressed their opinions, generally saying that the 9-cent slaughter tax has been in place for two years, and even the education subsidies are still in arrears. Other distributions are simply out of the question and should be donated to aviation for salvation. It was then decided that 30% would still be used for hygiene equipment expenses, and 70% would be used entirely for the aviation salvation fund. However, within the 70%, 600 yuan per month must still be set aside for education expenses until 100,000 yuan is reached. Before the 100,000 yuan is reached, the 9-cent slaughter tax will be kept by the Aviation Association, and several representatives from the meat industry will supervise the process. The Aviation Association will also send a letter to the municipal government, requesting that the Finance Bureau transfer all the remaining funds from the 9-cent slaughter tax over the past two years to the aviation salvation fund. The meeting then adjourned.

Ma Baoshan Candy and Biscuit Company Opens 195

Ma Baoshan Company was originally established in Hong Kong. Now, in order to expand its business, it has established a retail and wholesale business at Nos. 288-294 Xihua Road, Hongqiao. Its self-built steel and cement manufacturing plant is located behind the storefront. All kinds of candy and biscuit products are exquisitely made and delicious. They are all improved and manufactured by Mr. Ma Baoshan, the younger brother of the late pioneer Mr. Ma Yushan, with the knowledge and experience he gained in the past, and are praised by both Chinese and foreigners. It officially opened yesterday, and the guests were celebrities from all walks of life, including General Zhu Ziqiao, Lin Kanghou, Lao Jingxiu, Feng Shaoshan, Xiang Kangyuan, and hundreds of others. Mr. Ma Baoshan led them to visit the factory, and they praised the perfect equipment. It is reported that in order to thank customers for the opening, the retail department is offering a big sale for ten days.

Wu Chenghe's Funeral Today 196

Mr. Wu Chenghe, a wealthy silk and money merchant from Shaoxing, Zhejiang, who lived in Shanghai, was engaged in the silk and money business in Shanghai and made great efforts in exporting Chinese silk, directly selling Chinese silk to foreign countries. He founded many businesses and devoted himself to charity and public welfare, as well as to education in his hometown. He died at the age of 54. His son, Jin Cheng, is young and handsome and can carry on his father's business. Now that the mourning period for his father has ended, he has built a new tomb in Moushan Township, Yuyao, and the funeral of Mr. Wu and his wife, Mrs. Tian, will be held today (21st). Celebrities from all walks of life will either present inscriptions or attend the funeral. At that time, there will be plain cars and white horses, which will be a grand occasion.

Prepared Reserve Report Issued by the Four Banks Joint Treasury - No. 194 197

The Four Banks Joint Treasury is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu banks to exclusively handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with full reserves, with cash reserves of at least 60% and guarantee reserves of at most 40%. It is announced once a week and checked by the auditors of the four banks and accountants. The following is a transcription of the 194th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Treasury on September 16, 1933: Banknotes in circulation: 21,783,337 yuan. Total reserves: 21,783,337 yuan, including cash reserves of 18,044,537 yuan and guarantee reserves of 3,738,800 yuan. Zhabei

The Shanghai Huashang Public Bus Company has been operating the fourth stop on the first Shanghai-Jiangwan route at the entrance of the Parker Milk Company on Jiangwan Road. The content is rich and the price is especially low. The subscription for the whole year, including postage, is $1.20. It's doubled for foreign countries, but in order to give preferential treatment to national libraries, this publication only charges 50 cents for postage for domestic libraries to subscribe for the whole year. Lifestyle Bookstore, Modern Bookstore, and major bookstores in various places are selling it on consignment.

Shen Liangqin's Poems and Poetic Talks Published: Mr. Shen Gaoqin has always possessed talent and is also rich in learning. Recently, he printed and published the poems and poetic talks he has created. The works in this book are highly artistic and innovative. All writing about feelings and society is wonderful, and cannot be compared with the boring works of recent times. As for his poetic talks, he explains the principles and methods in many ways and can also say what others have not said. Those who want to study poetry must have a copy in their hands. Distribution points: Xidong Bookstore on Wuma Road, Shangwen Bookstore inside Xiaoximen.

*Law Journal, Constitution Special Issue* Published: The All-China Lawyers Association of the Republic of China has now compiled a book called (*Law Journal*) *Constitution Special Issue*. The content is divided into Liu Liumin's commentary on the first draft of the constitution, and also Xiao Buyun's philosophical view of constitutionalism, the spirit of political constitution and the spirit of economic constitution. Ruan Yicheng's view on the so-called localities in the future constitution, Hu Chongji's constitution and land issues, Chen Yaodong's discussion on the National Affairs Court, Liu Zhe's discussion on the economic committee in the first draft of the constitution, Sun Dexiu's critique of the first draft of the constitution of the Republic of China, Tian Heming's essays on the general provisions of the draft constitution, and the republication of the All-China Lawyers Association, the Standing Committee's words, and research reports on the draft constitution, etc. The text consists of tens of thousands of words and the second volume and first issue has been published. It is sold on consignment by the Shanghai Lawyers Association. The cost is 30 cents per copy. Also, a directory of the 1,037 new members of the Shanghai Lawyers Association, including the telephone numbers of the lawyers' lounges in each court, is printed to facilitate members' reference. It is said that many members have come to the association to collect them in recent days.

Weather Report 202

The Xujiahui Observatory predicted the weather at 4:30 PM yesterday: The sky is cloudy. The weather on the coast of Guangdong is bad due to a small hurricane southeast of Hong Kong, moving northwest. The hurricane north of Kyushu is moving northeast-east, and a low-pressure center is forming southeast of Japan. The southern coast of Japan has strong west-northwest to southwest winds. The hurricane between the Caroline and Philippine Islands is obviously moving northwest. The center of the hurricane southeast of Hong Kong was within 60 miles of the intersection of 22 degrees north latitude and 116 degrees east longitude at about 6 AM this morning. The one north of Kyushu was within 60 miles of the intersection of 35 degrees north latitude and 133 degrees east longitude at about 2 PM this afternoon. The wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was: highest 87.1, lowest 65.3; on the same day last year, the highest was 84.6 and the lowest was 67.1.

Fudan Defeats Hujiang to Win Men's Volleyball Championship 231

The City Games men's volleyball final between Fudan and Hujiang was held at 4:30 PM at the Chinese Athletic Field. Fudan's flying general, Cao Tingzan, returned to the field to lead the team. Although he was overweight and unable to jump and spike, his coordination of the team was very effective. As a result, despite Hujiang's strength, they had to concede defeat. The match was decided in four sets, with Fudan maintaining their dominant position as a perennial champion.

Fudan 21-11, 21-15, 19-21, 21-18 Hujiang

Fudan team wins Shanghai City Games volleyball championship (Photo by Qichang)

First Set, Fudan is Fierce 232

At the start of the match, Hujiang seemed flustered, and Fudan also had few special performances. After 6-6, Fudan's Cao Tingzan served fiercely, gaining the upper hand with an 11-7 lead. After switching sides, Fudan's momentum suddenly surged. Front row players Cheng Mingjue and Cao Tingzan were effective in blocking, and Qiu Guangxie took the opportunity to jump and spike, unstoppable. The score progressed to 17-7. Under the threat of Yan Li, Hujiang had little activity, and with their rear formation in disarray, Fudan won the set 21-11.

Second Set, Deadly and Effective 233

Starting in the second set, Fudan's Zhang Qunguang served, and their defense at the net was tight, leaving Hujiang with no opportunity to attack. The score became 9-3, with Fudan again gaining the advantage. Hujiang tried hard to rally, with Lu Kangyuan shouting encouragement, and they worked together to kill each point effectively, bringing the score to 7-9. However, Fudan still won the first half of the set 11-7. The situation became more intense after the change of sides, with Qiu Guangxie and Lu Kangyuan each showing their skills, going head-to-head. The ball flew back and forth like a cannonball, but Fudan always maintained the advantage, and Hujiang was unable to recover, with Fudan winning again 21-15.

Third Set, Hujiang Recovers 234

In the third set, Fudan still had the advantage, leading 11-6 in the first half, which seemed to create a situation where they would win the match in three straight sets. Unexpectedly, when Fudan was leading 18-14 and 19-16, their formation became disorganized, and Hujiang took the opportunity to attack, leaving Fudan with no chance to respond. Hujiang moved forward steadily and won the set 21-19, showing a resurgence and a promising momentum.

Fourth Set, Groping in the Dark 235

The third set ended, and the sun had already set. In the second half of the fourth set, the sky was already dark. Both sides groped in the dark, and the game became simpler. A successful kill was sure to score. Both sides made contributions in the tense first half, and the situation was very tight. Hujiang switched sides leading 11-10. However, after Fudan's Zhang Qunguang served, the score jumped ahead, with Fudan leading 16-12. Later, the score became 19-13. If they could score two more points, they could determine the victory. However, Hujiang did not relax, maintained a tight defense, and denied Fudan the opportunity to score. So after 20-16 (Fudan ahead), Fudan almost failed to add this valuable point. Hujiang reached 18-20, showing a situation similar to the previous set, coming from behind. Fudan had to work harder and finally won the final victory 21-18.

Cheng Mingjue, Xie Baochang, Cai Tiange

Fudan Lineup: Zhang Qunguang, Cao Tingzan, Zou Bingxin

Zhou Jieming, Qiu Guangxie, Chen Bofang

Two Soccer Games Yesterday 236

Jinan Wins Right to Finals, Donghua Wins Right to Replay

Two soccer games were held yesterday, one was the replay between Jinan and Xingguang, resulting in a 12-0 victory for Jinan, giving them the right to the finals. The other game was Donghua's 7-1 victory over Huahua, giving Donghua the right to a replay, which they will play against Youyou to compete for the right to the finals.

Jinan Defeats Xingguang: Jinan's lineup yesterday was completely new, with Yahui as the leading captain, Tan Di at the center, and Jiang and Gu guarding the two flanks. Xu Heng was in charge of the old camp. This lineup was a preliminary exercise for the finals. Xingguang's strength was far less than Jinan's, and their main players, Jiang Chao and Luo Douwen, deserted at the last minute, greatly weakening their strength. They fought with all their might in the first half, but still couldn't avoid losing four goals. In the second half, Jinan's players took advantage of the Xingguang goalkeeper's immature technique and adopted a long-range shooting strategy, firing from a distance and scoring every time. Liang Shutang, who had not fully recovered from his illness, sang his sick tune as if he was a treasure, and actually scored repeatedly, which was commendable. Xingguang failed to get close to the goal even once, losing twelve goals in a muddled and confused manner, which was also miserable.

Donghua Defeats Huahua: "Struggling like a mantis trying to stop a chariot, not ashamed even in defeat, like touching a tiger's whiskers and hurting your hand, defeat is also heroic." This is no different from a lament for Huahua yesterday. Huahua is a team organized by Shanghai merchants. In terms of strength, they are not as good as the top teams, but better than the bottom teams. Yesterday, they met the strong opponent Donghua, and knowing that they would lose, they were unwilling to surrender and be beaten, and the whole army swore to fight to the death, working together with all their strength to resist desperately. Even under the pressure of Donghua's sophisticated equipment and heavy firepower, they frequently launched counterattacks, which also managed to disturb Donghua's internal defenses, making people feel uneasy. It's just that Guan and Feng, like two earth elementals, under the leadership of Dr. Ju, had electric nets and lime bottles everywhere, making it difficult for Huahua to move an inch. Li Ning was as fierce as ever, wielding his big knife, and Fu Zhibin, Jia Youliang and others, although constantly probing east and west, found it impossible to find an opening. Five minutes before the end of the second half, Huahua had already lost seven goals, and everyone expected that Huahua would not escape the record of scoring zero eggs this time. Who knew that Huahua's counterattack would become even more urgent, and Dr. Tu made a slight mistake, allowing a leopard and wolf to enter the room. Jia Youliang passed the ball in front of the goal, and Huang Guorong arrived in time, smashing Fan's wooden door with a bang, making the score 7-1.

Judging Committee Organized 238

The rules of the Organizing Committee's Judging Committee are as follows: Article 1: This committee

shall be organized by the president with the appointment of five to seven members. Article 2: The powers of this committee shall be to judge and punish all protests concerning competitions and sportsmanship. Article 3: The decisions of this committee shall be final and no further protests may be made. Article 4: The president shall designate one member as chairman of this committee. Article 5: The meetings of this committee shall not be held on a regular basis and shall be convened by the chairman at any time. Article 6: The meetings of this committee must be attended by more than half of the members to be convened. Article 7: These rules shall be implemented after the resolutions of the City Education Bureau's Affairs Meeting.

Judging Committee Members: The City Education Bureau has appointed Ma Chonggan (Chairman), Chen Bai, Shao Rugan, Shen Siliang, and Zhou Jiaqi.

Men's Football Quarterfinals 261

Fifth District Wins Over Third District Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, the football quarterfinals were held. In the first match, the Fifth District played against the Third District in a fierce 90-minute battle. The Fifth District won convincingly with a score of 5-0. In the first thirty minutes, neither side scored. Later, the Third District's defense became weak. The Fifth District's center forward, Shen Fugeng, dribbled straight up, and from a short distance from the goal, his kick was slightly off, and the ball rolled towards the goalpost. The Fifth District then had a penalty kick opportunity, but they missed it by shooting too high. Shen atoned for his mistake by breaking through the defense, fearlessly charging straight into the enemy's territory, and the Third District lost a goal. This was the result of the first half. In the second half, although the Third District tried hard to counterattack, the Fifth District continued their efforts, scoring four more goals. In the end, the score was 5-0. The Fifth District won the right to compete in the final and will compete with the Second District for the championship.

Important News from the National Games 268

Funding for Participation of Mongolia and Tibet Settled (Nanjing, 20th) The organizing committee of the National Games believed that Hong Kong should have one unit, but both the South China Athletic Association and the Chinese Athletic Association of Hong Kong had athletes participating. It has replied by telegram requesting that they be combined into one unit to comply with the regulations. The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission informed the National Games that due to the inconvenient transportation in Mongolia and Tibet, it has instructed the Beijing offices of each league and banner to select athletes to participate. The Audit Department donated white yuan, the Accounting Department donated thirty yuan, and the Zhenwei Committee donated twenty yuan, requesting the National Games to produce prizes on their behalf.

Two Railway Administrations Plan to Open Special Trains between Beijing and Shanghai The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations previously received instructions from the Ministry of Railways that the 22nd National Games would be held in the capital during the Double Tenth Festival this year. They were instructed to add a passenger train from Shanghai to Beijing one day before the opening of the Games, and from Beijing to Shanghai one day after the closing of the Games. They immediately transferred the instructions to the Transportation Department for preparation. According to the report from the Transportation Department, (in accordance with the newly revised train timetable, and based on the speed of special express trains, it is planned to operate one passenger special train in each direction one day before the opening of the Games and one day after the closing of the Games. The northbound special train is scheduled to depart from Shanghai North Station at 17:00 and arrive in Nanjing at 23:25. The southbound special train is scheduled to depart from Nanjing Station at 7:20 and arrive in Shanghai at 14:09, but the passenger trains along the way may be slightly delayed due to the committee) and so on. The bureau has reported to the Ministry of Railways for instructions to be followed in accordance with Industry Letter No. 1660.

Executive Yuan Persuades Chen Bulei to Stay 269

(Nanjing, 20th) The Executive Yuan instructed to persuade Chen Bulei, the Director of Education of Zhejiang Province, to stay, saying, "We have received your report. Education in Zhejiang Province has always relied on your leadership. The nation is in the midst of difficulties, and we hope to work together. We hope that you will continue to shoulder the responsibility and work hard. We ask that you restrain your noble fatigue and take care of yourself. Your request to resign should not be discussed."
