Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn) - A literary column

Special Issue Untitled 270

—Shou Juan

Preface The reason why no special issue was published on the 918 Incident was not due to laziness, but rather to observe three minutes of silence. Now, on the third morning of this tragic anniversary, after the pain has subsided and we have had time to reflect, we suddenly have this special issue, called "Untitled." "Untitled" does not belong to the same category as those old poets who specialize in writing romantic poems, but rather it is like what the Buddha said, "unspeakable, unspeakable." This is the preface.

To Do 271

—Jun Ti

The anniversary of the September 18th Incident has passed. After the pain has subsided and we have had time to reflect, we should also ask ourselves: Our beautiful land was taken away by the enemy for no reason. Although the enemy is committing robbery, which is despised by humanity, they dare not commit this robbery against other countries, but they have committed it against us. Is this not our great shame and humiliation?

The beautiful land we lost was originally garrisoned by hundreds of thousands of troops; but the enemy who came to seize it only numbered a few thousand. Is this not our great shame and humiliation?

The beautiful land we lost has been gone for two years: In these two years, not only have we not been able to recover it, but we have continued to lose it. Is this not our great shame and humiliation?

Undoubtedly, this is our great shame—this is our great humiliation! We should not complain; nor should we blame others. So do not say that we are a naturally ill-fated nation; nor should we say that the League of Nations is not sincerely helping us: nor should we say that the government is not working hard; nor should we say that the military is not fulfilling their duties. The Republic of China belongs to all 400 million of our people. What we lost from our hands, we should recover from our hands. Those long sighs, calls for help, and begging for assistance are all signs of weakness.

We should dedicate our entire spirit and body completely; and we should combine the hearts of 400 million people into one. Then, if it is a matter of cultural work, no matter how beautiful or cheap the enemy's goods are, they cannot exchange for a penny from us; if it is a matter of military work, no matter how sharp or numerous the enemy's weapons are, they cannot defeat our 400 million people.

In other words, we should always do something, no matter what. There are two types of action, cultural and military. Cultural action means not buying the enemy's goods, and military action means fighting the enemy to the death.

My dear compatriots! Military action may require you to fight to the death, which you may be reluctant to do; cultural action not only does not require you to fight to the death, but also saves you money. Why are you unwilling to act fiercely even for this?

Night Ritual for the September 18th Incident 272

—Chen Liang

I got up early in the morning, without washing my face, and went alone to the hillside to pick a handful of yellow wildflowers and blood-red wildflowers to keep in water. That day, I didn't read or write, but just stayed in the corner of the room, with a sorrowful mood and sorrowful thoughts.

Silently waiting, waiting for the night to come. Night, as expected, came with a sad and gloomy face, and the autumn wind began to weep on the paper window. The old woman put the candlestick on the table by the window, and the flames kept jumping, making the room even more eerie.

So, I opened the door and ran out, carrying that handful of yellow and blood-red wildflowers.

Quietly, I quietly walked to the mass grave at the fork in the road, stopped, put down the flowers, and gave the mass grave a deepest salute. When I looked up, two lines of hot tears fell uncontrollably.

"The spirits of the martyred compatriots, perhaps you won't blame me for not bringing wine. Tonight, I offer you my sincere soul and this bouquet of nameless wildflowers. Since the night of September 18th two years ago, it has been exactly two years. Not only have we not recovered an inch of lost territory, but we have instead handed over tens of millions of square miles of land. The January 28th Incident in Shanghai added new wounds, and various hidden pains have occurred in North China. You must also be weeping in pain in the afterlife, right? It's not that we have failed your loyal and courageous sacrifice, but in reality, the environment makes us have a country that we cannot love, and blood that has nowhere to flow..."

Heartfelt Words 273

—Shou Juan

On the day of the September 18th Incident, there was a rain that shook the town. Although this was a change in the weather, perhaps it was the national soul of China wailing and crying! It was crying about the unworthy descendants of the Yellow Emperor, who have been sitting idly by and watching the territory of the Northeast fall for two years, and are still singing and dancing happily, as if nothing has happened.

As long as the hearts of a fallen nation are not dead, there may be a day to restore the homeland. Only a nation whose heart is dead will fall into a place of eternal doom. Even if the country has not fallen, it is more pitiful than a fallen nation. "At the entrance of Black Clothes Lane, the setting sun slants, it is the new ridge of another family." These lines describe the hatred of the fall of the Ming Dynasty. How profound and painful! Today, looking north with our heads raised, tears wet our clothes. Alas, our Great Wall has also become the new ridge of another family! I said to myself and started to sob and cry.

What exactly can we, the survivors, do for those martyred, loyal, and courageous soldiers and a group of innocent compatriots who suffered?

Insufficient Prevention 274

—Feng Moni

Yesterday, our housemate, Old Lady Zhang, suddenly started arguing and shouting at home, so I went over to listen. It turned out that Old Lady Zhang had come back from the street and saw a copper hanging ornament hanging in a second-hand store. After a careful look, it turned out to be something from her own home. How could it have been moved to a second-hand stall? She couldn't help but get angry, and rushed home in a rage, making a big noise without asking the reason, leaving her daughter-in-law confused. Later, according to her daughter-in-law, there was indeed this copper hanging ornament before, but because it was old, she had bought a new one to replace it, and put the old ornament aside. Now that she found it on a second-hand stall, she thought of the old ornament, so she wanted to investigate. Old Lady Zhang's reason for making a fuss was like this, but since she still wanted this old ornament, she should have paid attention beforehand. Only after she found it on a second-hand stall did she start making a fuss. However, no matter how much she made a fuss, the rights already belonged to the second-hand stall owner.

Not to mention a family like this, even the country is no different. Look, France occupies the Nine Small Islands, and Japan occupies the Eight Small Islands. Before they were seized by others, we never heard of the Nine Small Islands or the Eight Small Islands. Only after they were seized by others did we start making a fuss. However, no matter how much we made a fuss, the things were still seized by others. We should have taken precautions beforehand, so that we would not be coveted by others. The story of Old Lady Zhang is the same fact as our country's small island incidents.

Then, we Chinese have not only these few small islands, there are still small islands, and we should quickly prepare for the future. There is no need to only realize that they are our own things after they have been seized by others. You must know that things that have reached the hands of others are not easy to take back. It is ten times more difficult than digging a loach out of a cat's mouth. If we do not take precautions, no matter how much we protest after being seized by others, it will be of no avail. In fact, it is all because of insufficient prevention.

Melee by Ceng Shujuan 275

The desolate and gloomy wilderness, bleak and deserted, exposes a ferocious and vicious face: the stars and moon cover up their bright light, and a sinister and terrifying murderous aura shrouds the bleak universe.

The patriotic heroes with hot blood are all crawling in the damp trenches, holding their breath and tightly gripping their sharp swords, quietly waiting for the enemy's attack.

The enemy's field guns suddenly roared, exploding around the heroes; the enemy's planes suddenly dropped giant bombs, bombing near the trenches. Flesh and blood splattered with shrapnel, dust rolled with smoke, the pungent smell of blood, the piled up white bones, sadly exposed the cruelty of war in the hazy mist!

The wicked enemy, relying on its fierce firepower, invaded our heavily guarded positions. These brave and unparalleled warriors, with just a roar, seemed like mountains collapsing and cracking! Everyone leaped out of the trenches like dragons and tigers, rushing towards the enemy's core,衝击! But seeing white blades flying, cold light flashing, people falling and horses collapsing, red blood spurting; the enemy's heads fell with the sharp blades, and the enemy's blood splattered with the flashing knife light! In just an instant, this vast battlefield was already littered with corpses and blood-soaked fields!

The brutal enemy thought that a night raid would surely win a surprise victory; who knew that because of the melee by our loyal and courageous soldiers, they suffered deep pain. So whenever the pitch-black night came, they would deeply harbor the terror of death and dare not try the taste of these sharp white blades again.

This battlefield covered with corpses, this sinister and terrifying battlefield, because of the gift of this pungent melee, the enemy also shrank its covetous ambitions, and trembled, not daring to look directly. Therefore, this battlefield of bombing and slashing has transformed into a silent and calm wilderness: the bleak and gloomy air covers this gray universe like a net, and the light of the stars and moon cannot be seen.

Remembering the Homeland 276

—Chao Ye

Recovering from illness is like pulling silk, no different from sitting in a sorrowful city all day long. In my free time, I turned over and read the Notes from the Thatched Cottage of Close Scrutiny, and suddenly saw the following passage:

"I proofread the secret books and went to the Mountain Resort four times: in the winter of Dingwei, in the autumn of Wushen, in the summer of Jiyou, and in the spring of Renzi. I have seen all the beauty of the four seasons. Every time I sailed to the Wenjin Pavilion, the mountains and water were all natural, the colors of the trees and the sounds were all from a non-worldly realm. The weather, both sunny and overcast, morning and evening, was in a thousand states and shapes. Even a bird or a flower was all picturesque. What was even more extraordinary was that the fine grass along the slopes and valleys was all like green felt, no more than a few inches high, as neat as if it had been cut, with not a single stem that was uneven or of different lengths. The gardeners called it 'regulated grass.' Just a few steps out of the palace walls, the whiskers and tendrils are already spreading and growing. Isn't it true that heavenly plants are born to await the imperial遊哉?"

After reading it once, it struck me with horror! It was as if I were there. According to the Mountain Resort, it is outside Xifengkou, commonly known as the Rehe Palace. The scenery within has already been almost completely depicted in the 137 words on the right! Such a good place, meticulously planned and managed, with nature's workmanship, has unfortunately already been occupied by no more than 200 enemy soldiers, without even losing an arrow, who marched in formation and calmly took possession of it! From now on, for all of us Chinese people who want to travel here, besides reading this record and dream-travelling, what else is there to do but wait for its recovery? Remembering the homeland, I am extremely sad. Could it be that heavenly plants are born, not to await the 胡游, but must await the 夷游?

Broadsword Guan Xiong by Huang Kewei 277

On a main street in Beiping City, countless people were packed together. Police officers with white leggings weaved back and forth, using their black wooden batons to keep them off the street, clearing a wide path. They all stood on their tiptoes, craning their necks, looking outwards, but all they could see were heads: bristly, bald, wearing large bamboo hats, wrapped in white cloth...

The red sun cast down a ball of fire, and the sweat on their heads felt like it was boiling! Wisps of cooked air rose upwards, but they wanted to see the column of soldiers marching to their deaths with composure, showing no signs of weariness or fatigue. They waited, waited for the team that was risking their lives for the country and the nation to arrive.

(Look! Our soldiers are here!) A cry arose from the crowd. Then, everyone applauded in unison, cheering thunderously, like a clap of thunder.

A long, snake-like column finally marched into the street amidst the waving of tens of thousands of hands. They all wore blue silk turbans, black short jackets buttoned tightly, black leggings, and straw sandals. Broadswords with wide blades rested on their shoulders, gleaming and reflecting the sunlight. Red silk ribbons were tied to the swords, embroidered with two large characters: "Die誓死"!

Leading the column was a burly man with round eyes, a wide mouth, a purplish face, and a full beard that was greenish. This was Guan Xiong! He was silent, his facial muscles tense. They were leaving the realm of the living, advancing towards the path of death!

(Long live the Broadsword Brigade!) (Long live the Broadsword Brigade!) The words slipped from someone's mouth, resounding powerfully.

Guan Xiong's facial muscles twitched, and a faint smile appeared. His two pupils stared at the broadsword, as if saying to it: (Be brave, chop off a few more enemy heads!)

The straw sandals made a "thump-thump" sound, stepping over the cobblestones, mud, and rugged roads of the Shuimen River, and finally, they arrived at the front line. The dim night, the large moon buried in dark clouds, struggled. Struggled, a faint light slipped out, shining on Guan Xiong's gray face in the gray trenches. He tightened his wide belt, took a breath, and concentrated all his strength in his arms. He tested the broadsword, squatted down, and said to his comrades: (Our ancestor was Guan Yu關雲長. He relied on it to break the Yellow Turban rebels, slay Yan Liang, and execute Wen Chou, killing six generals. Our grandfather was Guan Sheng關勝. He also relied on it to suppress Liangshan Marsh. It has been passed down to our hands, so we have to bury ourselves in it. I am truly ashamed, I am sorry to this sword, and I am sorry to our ancestors.)

Boom! A "Sun Brand" shell whizzed over his head. His comrades quickly pulled him down to lie down. He touched his head and continued to squat, saying: (Tonight we will behead the enemy, let this sword that has not tasted meat for a long time taste something foreign.) As he spoke, a bright light circled in the sky. This was an airplane.

"Down!" the company commander shouted sharply. Two lightning-like searchlights shone down, followed by a huge bomb, flying down quickly.

Boom! Soil and stones danced, and the smell of gunpowder filled the trenches. Guan Xiong buried his nose in his knees, his blood boiling! (Damn it! Why haven't we charged yet?)

"Slow down! Hold your ground!" The cannons roared one after another, and the gunshots added to the chaotic clamor. Bullet-like missiles whistled as they flew from that side to this side, from this side to that side, drilling into the mud and into the bodies of the soldiers.

"Charge! Brothers!" Guan Xiong roared, pressed his broadsword into the ground, and jumped out of the trench. Then, the Broadsword Brigade, like fierce tigers, bravely charged forward!

The machine guns on the other side swallowed bullets and shook their heads, spitting them out at one group, but another group charged up, constantly, endlessly. Guan Xiong gritted his teeth tightly. He took a few steps closer, took out a hand grenade, and threw it. With a bang, the machine gun tilted its head, and half a dwarf leg flew in front of him. He grinned ferociously, pointed his broadsword, and shouted loudly: "Forward! Only by moving forward can we find a way out!"

Enemy soldiers poured out of the trenches, and then the two sides engaged in a melee. Snow-bright broadswords, bayonets, scarlet blood, bullets, severed heads, arms, thighs, screams, and shouts were all mixed together.

Guan Xiong. He swung his broadsword, killing wildly, using his ancestral flower sword with all his might. He defeated many enemy soldiers, but he also fell to the ground, exhausted.

The wolf-like sound of the machine guns gradually subsided, and the rising sun broke through the hazy mist, but revealed a face that was visibly mourning. At this time, Guan Sheng climbed up from the pile of corpses. He rubbed his eyes, looked at the enemy soldier beside him with half his brain cut off, and trembled as if he felt something. He picked up the broadsword with a broken blade, stepped on the bloodstains, stepped on the corpses, and ran towards the bright rising sun.

Jiangsu and Guangdong Corners Uneven 282

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

National Products Food and Drink Special Issue

Introductory Remarks

Confucius Was a Food Expert 303

— Yang Mang

Confucius was learned and all-knowing. Speaking of food and drink, plain water and simple meals seem very casual. But when you look into it, he really wasn't willing to be careless in the slightest. Things that were cut, if the shape wasn't right, he wouldn't eat them. (If it's not cut correctly, he won't eat.) He wouldn't eat vegetables without sauce. (If he can't get his sauce, he won't eat.) He wouldn't eat wine and meat casually bought on the market. (Cheap wine and market dried meat, he won't eat.) No matter what dish, ginger was indispensable. (He doesn't remove ginger from his meals.) When I was young and reading the "Village" chapter of the Analects, I often said to my teacher: "This Confucius is so particular about what he eats, no wonder Mrs. Confucius had a hard time serving this husband!" Everyone would burst into laughter. Look at the many things Confucius said, they are all inexplicably wonderful.

(1) "Food should be meticulously prepared, and minced meat should be finely chopped." Eating means eating hygienic rice. In other words, you have to eat some coarser rice. Brown rice is rich in vitamins, so rice is better the coarser it is. It can be seen that rice is based on the principle of coarseness. But when you go to someone's house to eat, then it is the time to make do, and one cannot dislike refined rice. In fact, how could he have liked eating refined rice? Coarse fish and big pieces of meat bring happiness to the mouth. It can be seen that the focus of cuisine is on proper cooking. If it is too small, it will never be refreshing or satisfying. But when going to someone's house for social occasions, one can only tolerate it and not dislike it. In fact, how could he have liked fine cuisine? (2) "Fish that is rotten or meat that is spoiled, he will not eat; food that is discolored, he will not eat; food that smells bad, he will not eat." Confucius's diet was extremely hygienic. If the fish was rotten, the meat was spoiled, or the dish was discolored or tasted bad, he would absolutely refuse to eat it. Now there are many restaurants that casually sell things that have been left overnight, truly deserving of death. If Confucius knew, he would definitely tell the little boys to beat the drums and attack them. (3) "If it's not properly cooked, he won't eat it." Confucius paid great attention to the art of cooking. Too raw is of course bad, but too cooked is also not good. A good bowl of vegetables, half-raw, is of course difficult to swallow, but if it is cooked until it is mushy and turns yellow, the vitamins have already been lost, and he would definitely shake his head and not eat it.

(4) "He does not eat what is out of season." Eating ice cream in winter or chrysanthemum hot pot in summer is of course out of season. There are also things like melons in April and May, and mooncakes in September and October, either the season hasn't arrived or it has already passed, and he wouldn't eat them.

In short, this Confucius was an extremely economical, extremely hygienic, and extremely scientific food expert. I think Mr. Xi, the boss of Guanshengyuan, as well as the managers and chefs in restaurants, should all study the Analects, or perhaps their products will be more popular.

Domestic Foods

Talking About Domestic Fish 304

— Ji Bo

"Fish" occupies a very important position in people's diet, with its freshness, deliciousness, and tenderness, its flavor is endless. Depending on individual preferences, cooking methods vary. There are also many local specialties, such as Songjiang perch, Yellow River carp, Jingjiang pufferfish, Jiading turtles, and Taihu triangular peaks (a type of carp), which are particularly talked about. "Fish" is delicious, as everyone agrees, the saying "big chunks of fish, big chunks of meat" shows that "fish" is considered a delicacy by gluttons. And the protein, vitamins, and lipids it contains are equal to or higher than those of duck, pork, chicken eggs, so its nutritional value is evident. Moreover, fish is rich in moisture, and the softness of its meat far exceeds that of birds and beasts. Not only can cooking save time, but digestion is also very quick, and the absorption of nutrients is easy. My country has the longest coastline and the widest fishing grounds, plus the Yellow River, the Yangtze River, and the Pearl River three major rivers cross several provinces, with many rivers and ports, and lakes and marshes scattered like stars. The abundance of fish is unparalleled in the world. The amount of supply is naturally in sight. The value of fish (in Shanghai), apart from some expensive varieties, is about the same as that of vegetables during the fishing season for small yellow croaker, large yellow croaker, blackfish, and ribbonfish, as well as various sturgeons. Fish has various conditions: nutritious, easy to digest, suitable for preferences, and affordable, and it is indeed a very important appetite-promoting side dish. Moreover, it is produced in our country's territorial waters and the Yangtze River. It is indeed a genuine national product. However, in recent years, "fish" of foreign origin have been mixed into the country from time to time. If the fence is built tight, wild dogs cannot get in!

Since we know that fish is important to people's lives, we should attach importance to the domestic fishing industry. Currently, my country's fishing industry is coveted by powerful neighbors. Foreign vessels intrude into our territorial waters and overfish, causing fish produced in our country to become imports. Although there are many national products in seafood and salted fish, they are also under pressure from foreign goods. The rivers in the interior should also be thoroughly investigated, (Japanese people come to China every year to investigate freshwater fisheries. Previously, there was Kensuke Kishigami investigating fish diseases and deaths in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River in Sichuan) with intentions of aggression, ambitious. If we do not take remedial measures, sooner or later we will sigh, "No fish to eat." When purchasing goods at national products companies and eating fish, readers should pay attention to whether the fish was caught by Chinese fishermen, very important, very important.

Understanding Tofu 305

— Zhen

Tofu, this is a purely domestic food and drink product. A Chinese student, Mr. So-and-so, once made countless profits from it overseas. Its history: the founder was Liu An, King of Huainan. Its raw materials are water and soybeans. Soybeans are plants rich in protein, so tofu's nutrition, though slightly inferior to meat and eggs, is superior to milk. The absorption of protein is (96%) for tofu, (93%) for milk, and (98%) for meat and eggs. A piece of tofu weighing two kilograms has a life force of 128 grams of protein, 68 grams of fat, 14 grams of carbohydrates, and can generate 1190 calories, nearly half of the daily calorie requirement. Therefore, tofu is a truly nourishing food. Moreover, the "Compendium of Materia Medica" also says that tofu, in addition to being clear and lovely, can broaden the middle, benefit qi, harmonize the spleen and stomach, eliminate distension, remove turbid air in the large intestine, and clear heat and blood, so tofu also acts as a medicine.

Although tofu is our daily food, many people may not know its method of preparation. Actually, it is very simple, but to make it white and tender, the effort is not easy. First, soak soybeans in water for ten hours, or four or five hours in summer. Then, grind them into a fine powder and slurry with water in a mill. Filter it with cloth to obtain raw soy milk and soybean residue. Soybean residue can be used as pig feed. Put the raw soy milk into a wok and simmer it over low heat. When it reaches over 300 degrees, the milk is cooked. A thin layer can be obtained on the surface of the wok, called tofu skin, which is the most nourishing among tofu products. Cooked milk is soy milk. Add gypsum to the milk to coagulate it into soft tofu, or tofu pudding. Pour it into a cloth bag and squeeze it with external force to obtain dried tofu, dried bean curd shreds, and other products. The amount of water it contains depends on the amount of squeezing force applied. If alum instead of gypsum is used to coagulate it, the poured tofu is tofu. Tofu is best made tender, so a pressure of about 80 kilograms is suitable. If it exceeds that, it will become old, and if it is less, the tofu will not set. The duration of time must also be noted. The above is a general outline of the method of making tofu. There are other recipes for eating it, so there is no need to say more. Speaking of its nature, in addition to the above-mentioned effects, its surface can be praised for being soft and white, and its taste is truly noble compared to the sea food from enemy countries. Fellow countrymen, may you never forget this completely domestic, economical, and nourishing food.

National Products Talk

Talking About National Products Foods 306

— Ba Ling

Clothing, food, housing, and transportation are the four major elements of life, and food ranks second, showing its importance. Now there are many people who, when they talk about food, always think of eating big dishes or foreign things, as if not eating foreign things is related to their own face. This is really a wrong idea, and we should correct it. We are Chinese and should use Chinese goods. Of course, eating is no exception. Since we are Chinese, we should eat national products foods and never have the idea of valuing foreign goods and belittling domestic products. You must know that the imperialist aggression against China is meticulous. In terms of food alone, a lot of money is taken away from them every year. Therefore, we should quickly wake up. Everyone should develop the habit of using national products this year. That is an urgent matter.

As for national products foods, there are really many now, and they have also made a lot of progress compared to before. Compared with foreign goods, they are on par and keeping pace. Take Guanshengyuan's foods, everything is domestic: mooncakes, fruit preserves, minced meat... There are many items, too many to list. The things are good and the prices are not expensive. We should rise up and promote them. So that domestic food becomes better every day.

There are also biscuits from Taikang Company, etc., which are all authentic domestic foods, known to everyone. Why shouldn't we eat domestic foods?

In short, in the National Products Year, we should use Chinese goods. Now we can change these two sentences for the time being: "In the National Products Year, we should eat Chinese goods." Readers, do you think this is right?

National Products Discussion

Advocating Domestic Horticulture Cooperation 307

— Wei Zhong

The market is full of various kinds of imported fresh fruits, as well as fruit juice, jam, and other fruit products. The annual outflow of funds is more than huge sums. In 1920, I also founded a six-mu orchard in my hometown. On the one hand, it was for my own interest, but soon I gained rich profits. So I immediately attracted people's attention. In just a few years, orchards could be found everywhere nearby.

But it became a flash in the pan, just like Chinese people starting a new business. This prosperous phenomenon of the emerging horticultural industry eventually declined and fell due to inconvenient transportation, blocked sales channels, poor cultivation, inferior products, and lack of attention to packaging and manufacturing. Fruit trees, which were once considered gold trees, are now cut down for fuel. Mu of orchards are still turned into crop fields. How long ago did this change occur? Looking back on the past, I can't help but feel the changes in time!

Is the horticultural industry at its end? But aren't thousands of imported oranges, tangerines, coconuts, as well as semi-finished and finished products such as raisins, fruit juice, and jam, filling our markets everywhere? This is definitely not the end of horticulture, but the decline of the horticulturalists themselves!

To save the current trend of decline in the domestic horticultural industry, of course, this cannot be ignored. We can only find the source of the disease, prescribe the right medicine, which is roughly nothing more than: one, improving cultivation methods, two, engaging in sorting and packaging, three, finding ways to facilitate transportation and open up markets, and four, establishing factories for manufacturing, storage, and extraction.

But how easy is this to say? Without a large amount of capital and without considerable talent, it is impossible to do it. To adapt to the current environment, I believe that the (cooperation) method is the most suitable.

Undoubtedly, we must immediately gather all comrades who are engaged in horticulture or interested in horticulture and organize a (horticultural production and sales cooperative) to concentrate our capital and talent to jointly engage in the improvement and development of horticultural production, transportation, sales, and manufacturing. In this way, we may be able to save one ten-thousandth of the huge annual outflow of funds on imported fruits.

New Industry Introduction

A Record of Yangfen Manufacturer Liang Daoyuan 308

— Gong Bai Ju

Yangfen, sold in grocery stores in the market, is made from seaweed called agar, which is produced in the sea. This powder is a specialty of Japan. Annual sales to the Chinese mainland are nearly millions of yuan, accounting for an important part of its country's exports. During the Republic of China era, Mr. Liang Daoyuan from my hometown, after investigating the Haiyang County area, found that it produced a very rich amount of agar. The fishermen did not know how to make powder and abandoned it. Therefore, Mr. Liang prepared funds and went to Japan to learn the method of making powder. He soon learned it and returned to China. He immediately founded the Rushan Yangfen Company in Haiyang and personally supervised the construction. The powder produced was pure white and better than Japanese goods. Just as he was promoting and developing, there were unscrupulous elements among the shareholders who intended to seize power and engage in private interests. Mr. Liang resigned in extreme anger. However, the company was also dissolved as a result. Later, in the winter of 1915, I met Mr. Liang in Tianjin. He still intended to start collecting capital and set up a factory again. I ran around and advocated for it, but in the end, because I was of low status and my words carried little weight, it was called off due to lack of responses. A few years ago, I read in the newspaper that Mr. Liang had already set up a factory in Jinan. It is said that the capital was provided by the government. However, Mr. Liang is always enthusiastic about China's industry, and he is frugal, capable, and particularly skilled. Moreover, this kind of industry is a pioneering concept in the country. The development of his business can be predicted.

Random Notes from Bushu Studio (1) 309

— Rong Yu

Prelude

I live in the countryside of Jiangwan, in a tile-roofed house up and down, facing a vegetable garden of over an acre. Although it is not as crowded as the Shanghai shikumen, a small living room is where the children roll around and jump; my wife sews and mends; and I write and read, with no other place to go. Is such a place worthy of being called a studio? However, literati like to put on a show and always inscribe a studio name to amuse themselves. I cannot be an exception. Should I inscribe about wind, flowers, snow, and moon? People would ridicule it as decadent. Should I inscribe about expelling the barbarians and honoring China? I dare not boast of such a big mouth. After thinking again and again, I had an idea! The scenery in front of me can be borrowed as the studio name. Small characters (family four days, all wearing Dayou clothes: home-cooked vegetables, often chewed, then call it (Bushu Studio)!) Gentlemen, don't underestimate these two words, Bushu, genuinely domestic products, completely local products, with no counterfeiting or mixing at all! What kind of writing should be written in this studio? Please see the text below:

Zongzi Candy and Chocolate 310

When children have nothing to do, they always like to chew on things. They don't want sour or spicy things, they just reach out their little hands and ask for candy. When they are crying so hard that tears and snot are flowing, as long as you put a piece of candy in their mouths, they will turn from crying to laughing, giggling with their little mouths, jumping around and playing. Candy is really the only lover of children!

Whenever Mao Tou from the east neighborhood cried, his parents would spend a copper coin to buy a zongzi candy and put it in his mouth, and he would leave smiling. The young master from the west neighborhood chewed chocolate all day long. According to his nanny, chocolate costs seven jiao and a half a pound, and he chews one or two pounds a day!

Time passes very quickly. In an instant, Mao Tou, who ate zongzi candy, wears cloth clothes; chews on vegetable roots, and has risen from an apprentice to the manager of a store. The young master from the west, who eats chocolate, wears a suit; eats foreign food; goes to dance halls, and has fallen into the group of "thieves". Everything starts from family education. Don't despise this zongzi candy! Therefore, Hu wrote a song:

Zongzi candy, sweet and delicious, you don't need silver to buy it, children treasure and cherish it. This is a domestic product; this is our own people, keep one in your mouth often, and spring will be in the room.

Chocolate, the taste is new; fragrance lingers on the lips, it is truly a treasure on the table. First, I sigh at the expensive price; second, I sigh that it is a foreign product. When it enters the mouth, it also disappears, and the money turns into dust.

Local Products Introduction

Ham 311

— Chuan Jingjia

Speaking of ham, everyone thinks of Jinhua. Jinhua's ham is indeed very famous. I am fortunate to be born in a place that produces ham, so at least, seeing ham won't make me consider it a treasure like people from other places.

Although ham is said to be produced in Jinhua, the production areas should also include Dongyang and Yiwu. There, ham is the largest product, and the amount shipped out each year is countless! In recent years, other businesses have been losing money, only the ham business is relatively good, so there are even more people doing ham business!

Even though it's just a small ham, it takes a lot of time, effort, and strength. First, the pig leg must be cut off, then it is cured with salt. It also needs to be sun-dried and washed, and the bad fatty meat on the leg has to be cut off. It really takes a lot of effort.

The taste of ham is truly indescribable. Just the bright red color is enough to make people drool.

Of course, other places also have cured legs, but the taste is always better with Jinhua ham. This is not because Jinhua has some special "feng shui" for producing ham, it is simply because the pigs in that area are raised well. There, raising pigs is the biggest side income for farmers. On the one hand, they rely on pig manure for fertilizer, and on the other hand, they can earn money. They don't raise pigs casually; the pigs' feed is even better than people's food. Barley, beans, sweet potato leaves, etc., are common feed. Many families mix glutinous rice or other human food into the pigs' feed. Therefore, because of the different feed, the meat of the pigs there is somewhat different, so the taste of the ham is more delicious.

Talking about Wuxi's Local Products 312

— Zhang Mengzhao

*Shenbao* is publishing a special issue on domestic food and beverages. I am gathering materials, so let me talk about the local products of (Nanyi) Wuxi. If people from other places and regions all make honest contributions about their local scenic foods and beverages, we can naturally defeat foreign flavors.

Oil Gluten 313

Wuxi gets the beauty of mountains and rivers. The man-made specialty, oil gluten, has a round outline, is moist and soft, and has a unique flavor when cooked properly. Visitors to Wuxi must buy it. Wuxi Sanle Company also has exquisitely packaged canned gluten, which will not spoil for a long time. It is especially delicious as a side dish.

Meat Bones 314

(Everyone knows to buy Wuxi meat bones to eat). The fame and deliciousness of meat bones can be imagined. However, to get fine-skinned, white-fleshed, well-cooked spareribs, the one from "Liang Tou Sanfeng Bridge" is second to none. Other meat shops such as Dashiqiao Tantoushu are also good.

Osmanthus Chestnuts 315

The golden breeze sends coolness, and the fragrance of osmanthus gradually permeates. Wuxi's famous osmanthus chestnuts are about to hit the market. The golden yellow flesh is tender and smaller than the Liangxiang chestnuts. In recent years, there have been many imitations. Real osmanthus chestnuts are produced in front of the Niangniang Temple in Huishan. The price is relatively high, costing one yuan for two catties, which may not be enough. Demand exceeds supply, so it is naturally expensive. If we take good varieties and cultivate and produce them well, their richness and nutrition can defeat cod liver oil and wheat flakes.

Honey Lin Aldehyde 316

A kind of honey lin aldehyde in Wuxi wineries is sweet, moist, and not dry, clear and lovely. Drinking too much will only cause slight drunkenness. It is enough to defeat imported wines and beers. It is a pity that the people of Wuxi do not decorate and develop it, and sit idly by while the rights and interests are taken away, which is truly regrettable!

Students' Domestic Breakfasts 317

— Mu

The extravagance of student life is recognized by all walks of life, especially in Shanghai. Now, I want to say based on facts that student life is not necessarily extravagant, especially when it comes to breakfast. The food that students eat is mostly economical for the common people. Of course, these foods and beverages are completely domestic products. Let the reporter introduce them one by one on the left.

(1) Baked sweet potatoes: This food is a genuine local product, a pure domestic product. Its nutrition is known for being rich in carbohydrates. (2) Cifàn: Cifàn is made by steaming glutinous rice over water. It is glutinous and rich in nutrition. When selling it, the scattered grains must be gathered and kneaded with a towel to form a melon shape. Usually, forty or fifty cents will get you a dense ball that is enough to fill you up.

(3) Fried steamed buns: They are a very small kind of steamed bun, worth twenty cents. The shell is made of flour, and the filling is minced meat or bean paste, and fried in oil until cooked. It is quite delicious and filling. (4) Soup noodles: This is a well-known domestic food and beverage. Although the price may be higher at times, it is quite cheap in itself. Sometimes, a dozen copper coins can get you full.

(5) Tofu soup: The value of tofu soup is well known to the Chinese people. It is not only nutritious, but the various items mentioned above are all food, while tofu is a beverage. Forty cents for tofu soup plus a copper coin for sugar is cheap and good, isn't it great? In addition to the various breakfast foods and beverages mentioned above, other items such as milk, coffee, bread, and Western pastries are not economical foods and beverages, and are mostly foreign goods. Even the porridge that we must have is not dared to be listed, because we don't know if it is Annam rice or Siamese rice.

— Xiao Bai

Mooncakes are the most historically valuable and poetic thing in our country. When the new moon hangs high in the sky, and the brand-new signboards in the streets reflect "New Mooncakes on the Market", we meet with it after a long separation. Once a year, we naturally feel extra close and lovely.

At this time, the China National Products Company, our national product headquarters, also held a large (Mooncake Assembly). It brings together the most famous mooncakes from various places, mainly divided into (Ning style), (Su style), and (Guang style), with hundreds of different sizes and types of fillings. It is truly an unprecedented initiative.

At this time, looking at the bright moon and chewing on sweet mooncakes is both pleasant, cheap, and also considered promoting domestic food and beverages, so why not do it!

Silver Ear Fungus Composition and Nourishing Effects 319

— Tiancheng

Every time autumn and winter arrive, we eagerly think about taking tonics, because we have been working hard for a year, and our bodies and minds are inevitably damaged. We should have something to nourish ourselves. The well-known tonics include ginseng, deer antler, bird's nest, and silver ear fungus. However, most people are ignorant of the specific nourishing qualities they contain and their effects, only knowing that ginseng nourishes qi, deer antler has a hot nature that separates it from ginseng, and bird's nest nourishes yin. They know relatively little about the effects of silver ear fungus, such as treating yin deficiency, weak constitution, lung disease, hemoptysis, chronic cough, gastritis, constipation, hemorrhoids, female metrorrhagia, leucorrhea, indigestion, and other symptoms. According to the effects of the above-mentioned tonics, ginseng, deer antler, and bird's nest are simple and have weak and biased effects. Silver ear fungus (i.e., white fungus) has the most uses and is most suitable for our consumption.

Although the uses of silver ear fungus are as described above, they are based on the word-of-mouth of elders, which is believed to be true. Now that science is flourishing, we should verify it in practice and know its composition before we can regard it as accurate.

The Sichuan stores in this city are famous for specializing in Sichuan silver ear fungus. The store previously invited Hu Zejun of the Chinese Science Society to conduct accurate scientific verification on the silver ear fungus produced from its own mountain fields in Sichuan. The results of the verification showed that silver ear fungus contains a large amount of fat, protein, *, *, iron, sodium, and other elements, and even more mucilage similar to gum arabic. Medical experts say that this mucilage has three major effects: (1) aids digestion, (2) replenishes blood, and (3) facilitates bowel movements (according to doctors during the European War, people who lost too much blood on the battlefield used 6% gum arabic and 0.7% salt added to distilled water to inject into blood vessels to fill the blood, with good results. Please refer to the book *Research on Sichuan Silver Ear Fungus* published by the Chinese Science Society).

It is said that Sichuan silver ear fungus can cure all diseases and prolong life if taken for a long time. Now, looking at the ingredients it contains, it is not an empty word. No food can simultaneously have the above three functions, and it is even more difficult to find in tonics. Now that silver ear fungus has all of them, it deserves the title of rare treasure.

It is found that the production area of silver ear fungus is not only Sichuan, but also Guizhou and Hubei provinces. Due to the different geographical climates, the efficacy seems to be less than that of Sichuan. Therefore, sellers all call it Sichuan silver ear fungus.

— Zhizhong

The most fashionable domestic food on the market now is none other than mooncakes. Furthermore, think about whether all parts of our country can be full of people, every family reunited, and eat these mooncakes peacefully year after year.

Free Talk

Books for Women to Read 322

— Xu Maoyong

Recently, there are too many books for children to read. Regardless of the quality, just looking at the quantity, we can say: "Our children are blessed."

However, I think we still lack a type of book: books for women to read. Originally, women are also people, and there is no need to separate everything from men ("bridges go to bridges, roads go to roads"). However, due to traditional relationships, the footsteps of today's women mostly cannot directly walk on the single-plank bridge, so we must build another road for them. The facts are there, and no one will deny it. However, our cultural circles do not seem to have noticed this. If they can't cross the bridge, they are left on the other shore. This kind of laissez-faire policy will inevitably hinder the development of culture. As Chugawa Hakuson said well: "The relationship between men and women in cultural life is like a three-legged race. No matter how well one side can run, it will not succeed if the other side cannot run."

Previously, there were indeed periodicals such as *New Woman* and *Women's Magazine*, as well as the series of books from the *Women's Issues Research Association*, but they were all selected to conduct academic research on women's issues. It is difficult to know how these books affect women, but as far as I can see, it seems that men read these kinds of books more, and the impact is also greater on men. Now, let's not talk about that for now. I just want to say that in addition to these kinds of books, women also need a kind that provides general knowledge in a special style, so that slightly educated women can never tire of reading it, gradually improve their insights, and cultivate their understanding and judgment of things.

Just like with children, I think a special style is also needed for women.

As for the general modern ladies, it is still best to provide multi-angled love novels. It is said that the French perfume king Coty (François Coty) started as a perfume merchant entirely by mastering the three principles of women's psychology: First, the name of the perfume must be pleasing to the ear; second, the bottle must be exquisite; third, the price must be expensive. Our publishers can follow these three principles: First, the name of the book must be pleasing to the ear; second, the cover must be exquisite; third, the price must be!! No, this one must be modified: the price must be cheap. Because our modern ladies want to save their money to buy expensive perfumes.

In the magazine called "Joke", I saw these words: "Jin Yan, a star who is loved by many ladies because of his gentle smiling face and various conditions suitable for women of the leisure class, should change his role after *Mother's Light* and give the ladies meaningful guidance and lead them to the path of light. Ladies have some idol concepts, and they will not leave Jin Yan because of his changing role, so he does not need to deliberately abandon them."

This is also a way of putting new wine in old bottles, which our love novelists have tried, but the success seems to be far less than that of *Mother's Light*. There are other reasons for this, which I think are unrelated to the essence of the method. The author of *Spring Silkworms*, in a sense, is also a user of this method, but the influence of this author is mostly still on men. For women, another kind of writer is needed. This section is just about literature.

Street Sketch 323

— Peng Xuezhen

On Saturday afternoon, XX Street is, as usual, crowded like a small fish pond with many fish. People pass through it diagonally, some stopping to look at the shop entrances, others walking forward like rushing records, stumbling and bumping.

Because it is just the beginning of the semester, the streets are full of students. The male students' light-colored jackets or turned-down collar shirts, young and light footsteps, are mixed with laughter. The female students' white shirts and short skirts fluttered smartly in the west wind, and some had triangular badges hanging on their collars. Rickshaw pullers approached them:

"Want a rickshaw, Panmen?" If they guessed correctly, they smiled with their mouths open. In the bookstores, female students asked for discounts in sharp voices, picking out some exquisite new-style stationery. They also always forgot to go to foreign goods stores to buy some Dream Cream or Simon Cream. Young hearts always love beauty, although they sometimes asked, "Isn't this soap box Japanese?"

Advertisements for "Tianjin Liangxiang" and "Various Mooncakes on the Market" attracted many people, who stretched out their hands and waited patiently. Beggars chased behind the men, shouting, "Young master, cultivate blessings and longevity, go abroad in the future, become an official..." Behind the women, they said, "Do good deeds, miss, marry a rich and powerful chairman, military commander in the future..." Disappointed, they turned around and mumbled, "Don't you want luck!"

The traffic police stood at the crossroads, waving their batons, sometimes knocking on the rickshaw awnings. When they were in a bad mood, they grabbed a few rickshaw cushions and dragged them to the police booth. The rickshaw pullers showed pitiful but angry eyes, and ran away before the baton slipped onto their backs. The wheels rattled on the cobblestone streets.

But a city without trams and cars is always quiet. The bells and horns of chartered rickshaws were drowned out by the mixed voices of the people, becoming such a vague and noisy piece. There was no shocking stimulation. The sounds released by the radio were also ordinary, mostly storytelling or songs like "Baby Wants to Sleep."

A group of people disappeared into the streets and alleys, and another group of people poured out from the streets and alleys. The cool autumn breeze carried the fragrance of women, and everyone felt a slightly drunk and refreshed mood.

Autumn 324

— Mei

I woke up in the middle of the night, the rain sound was monotonously pattering, and the wind was calling whirringly at the corner of the house. "Autumn is here again," I suddenly remembered.

The glass window was trembling like this, the lamp was silently silent, and a triangular small room was rippling with the desolate taste of the new autumn night. I lay down, lying down so that my bones felt sore everywhere. This is the usual state of rheumatoid arthritis patients on rainy nights, which I didn't mind. I opened my hazy tired eyes and looked around, and everything around was so dead! Covered with a thin blanket, I felt a slight cold on my skin, and I was sure: "Autumn has indeed arrived in the world," and I knew this was the bleak autumn night.

Time is really flying fast like an arrow. I remember one hot summer evening, after watching a play performed by my friends at the Russian Little Theater, I left the theater late at night and went to a ship berthed at the Shiliupu Pier. That was a summer night with the moon shining brightly on the waves and the sea breeze blowing away the heat. I said goodbye to Shanghai, where I had lived for a long time, and to all my dear friends, and threw myself into the arms of my hometown, which I had not seen for seven years.

At that time, my heart contained the joy of fantasy and the bitterness of reality, which was the so-called bittersweet situation. On one side, I was always reluctant to leave Shanghai and my friends in Shanghai, and on the other side, I was looking forward to everything in my hometown. My mood on the way home was truly unspeakably contradictory, apprehensive, apprehensive, until I arrived home.

Naturally, after seven years of separation, it cannot be said that the appearance of my hometown has not changed at all. At least, it is a fact that there is an extra Zhongshan Park and a clock tower. Although the park is reconstructed and not very good: the clock on the clock tower is also inaccurate. This is the achievement of the so-called "construction" that the people of the whole county spent a lot of money to obtain after the revolution, according to the people of my hometown.

I wanted to take advantage of the leisure of this summer vacation to stroll around as much as I wanted, and I had already planned on the way home to visit various places of interest. Who knew that I didn't realize it in the end, because the disease entangled me again. I lay down almost every day without moving, and did nothing except occasionally go to the fields to see the farmers harvesting rice and turning waterwheels. I really tasted the pale taste of rural life, which often made me recall my childhood, and suddenly I returned to my original life.

Unexpectedly, a long summer vacation was spent silently in illness and boredom. It seemed that time was particularly short. In a flash, I fell into autumn again. At the same time, I bid farewell to my dear family and friends again, sitting on the boat that had taken me home, quietly floating with the merciless seawater to Shanghai, which I had not left for a long time. Because it had not been long since I left, Shanghai and I did not feel unfamiliar at all.

The road was full of signs for autumn sales, and the women had also changed into thin autumn clothes. The whole city smelled of autumn. "Autumn is here." This is thousands of times, and it will never deceive people.

Really! Now is the time when summer is going and autumn is coming, and people's moods are also changing from hot to gloomy! With this gloomy mood, I happened to encounter this merciless wind and rain, which made a few hints of gloom. People wandering in a foreign land really don't know how to be comfortable? This little heart was finally gripped by gloom, gripped tightly.

Autumn! Don't be gloomy anymore, how good it would be if it cleared up tomorrow! I prayed like this in a low voice!

However, the rain was still pattering outside the window, and the wind was still calling whirringly. Still, I was also worried about the gloom of tomorrow!

Organizing Books 325

— Tang Tao

Let's start with a commonplace remark: the autumn air is cool after the rain, perfect weather for reading.

I've just moved, and my room is like a cage. It can't hold many books, but I still have four boxes in disarray, so I have to organize them myself.

The books are a mix of Chinese and Western, ranging from poetry, essays, novels, and the Bible, to Zuo Zhuan, Spring and Autumn Annals, and many works ending in "-ism", down to Jade Calendar Excerpts, Guanyin Precious Scrolls, Complete Book of Fortune Telling, and How to Write Letters Without Asking for Help. I have a little of everything. It makes me happy to bring these sages and scholars, and these charlatans trying to make a living, together in one place, spending dawn and dusk together.

So I began to organize.

Each of these books took its own stand, shouting and arguing loudly, showing off its own special skills to win my trust. Confucius advocated the way of the king, Zilu promoted military force, Dante sang of divine comedy, Shakespeare wrote grandly like a stingy miser, the ghost of impermanence catches people in broad daylight, Guanyin Bodhisattva saves all living beings, the fortune teller shakes his five fingers, calculating back and forth, and concludes that you have a good fate after all, which does not match the facts; Later, one is missing metal from the five elements of wood, water, fire, and earth, a lucky star shines high, and a decade of luck is ruined, causing one to exclaim in despair!

At this point, the fortune teller bore the brunt of the attack. Because I found his skills to be really poor. I decided to put the Complete Book of Fortune Telling and Evolution and Ethics together, so that he could get some Western education, learn a few ABCDs, and become Westernized in the meantime.

Unexpectedly, Confucius refused to accept this, spouting nonsense and claiming that this was "using barbarians to change Xia," and only a traitor would be so insane! This statement angered me so much that I plucked out all of his beard hairs, leaving not a single one. After staring closely, I found that he had turned into a pretty boy. Serves you right, who told you to be so fiercely moralistic!

Just then, my friend X came to visit. X is a graduate of a certain church university. After he came in and took a careful look, he quickly hid the Bible behind his back, and pointed to the Guanyin Precious Scrolls and said to me, "In the twentieth century, you are still so superstitious, aren't you afraid people will laugh their heads off?" I blushed with shame and suddenly realized my error. I scolded the Guanyin Bodhisattva severely, and she had to let her hair down, walk barefoot, cover her face and weep, and stride off towards the Flaming Mountains.

I repeatedly praised my friend X's achievements. X became complacent and bumped Shakespeare's knee. Shakespeare was furious and displayed his theatrical skills of using fake knives and spears, thrusting diagonally with a knife. Unexpectedly, he stabbed X in the backside. With a thud, the Bible fell to the ground, and (my friend) fell head over heels. All the books that had been organized were knocked over, and half a day's work was wasted.

Oh well! I'll wait a few days before organizing again.

Stimulation 326

— Xie Bing

If there is one person, I think he must have moments of seeking stimulation | at least once or twice in his life. After Gou and Hao left, I suddenly felt lonely, not wanting to say a word all day, not wanting to see anyone, only wanting to be alone, eating alone and singing alone. However, it was too strange. When they were here, I felt too unfree, too troublesome, even just going out casually, they would ask:

"Bing, where are you going?"

As for drinking boiled water, eating candy, and eating peanuts, it goes without saying, they always gave me some first. One day I wanted to write a letter, and they also wanted to write in their diaries, but the small table was piled with things, and it was difficult to write, so I hated them a little: | | Leave, it would be great if you left.

But this thought only lasted for a moment, and I immediately realized my mistake.

| | They finally came here, and you spent more than half a month to welcome them. Why are you arguing over something as small as sesame seeds?

So, taking advantage of Gou asking me "Is it easy to write?", I hurriedly put on a smiling face and answered her:

"Easy to write, easy to write!"

Also, night was the time I hated the most.

In the small room, there was a bed made of a few pieces of wood and a small table, which was already so crowded that three people couldn't turn over, and adding a folding bed made it even more impenetrable. The folding bed was so bulky and difficult to handle, and sometimes three people couldn't manage it, and Hao and my hands were often cut by the nails. Therefore, I once hated them:

| | Leave, it would be great if you left.

But the dreaded day finally came, they really left!

The day before they were about to leave, although I was busy writing a few letters to ask them to take to Shanghai, my heart was very calm, as if they weren't going to leave. The telephone number of whether the sedan carriers were available didn't come, and I thought there was no hope.

| | They won't be able to leave, I'm just calling the sedan carriers to trick them.

I proudly and firmly believed. (To be continued)
