Discussions

(Anti-War) and (War Preparation) Jian 327

Recently, news of both extremes are being simultaneously revealed in the same newspaper: one is that the World Anti-War Conference is closing in some location: the other is that the great powers are also scheming and struggling against each other, exerting themselves to prepare for war.

The representatives of the Anti-War Conference are being subjected to (detention) and (prohibition from landing) everywhere. The meeting place, (a slap in the face by the authorities of a certain concession): (the attitude of the National Government) is (still uncertain); whether or not they can obtain a "permit" for holding the meeting within the concession for the sake of Sir Eric Drummond's personal nationality and face is also (still uncertain), I'm afraid?

Turning around to look at the countries preparing for war, it is lively and extraordinarily tense: the United States wants to complete its warship plan, the Italian air force visits the United States, the French air force flies to the Soviet Union, Britain is rushing to build the Singapore naval base and making more fighter jets. The Soviet Union is even more on edge and confronts its neighboring countries, brandishing its swords. In addition, Japan, a nation that has gone war-mad, is increasing military spending, expanding its power, conducting air defense drills, and especially flaunting its naval maneuvers, being arrogantly invincible. Even the Soviet Union, with a different political system, is also busy with military preparations: small countries such as Belgium are also eager to build solid defense works on the border, filled with fear and anxiety.

On the anti-war front, it is almost impossible to find a place to meet, even though the earth is vast: on the war preparation front, the momentum is huge, and the air is towering. Although this defense force is heavily fortified and facing each other, if one compares the actual strengths, (anti-war) is like piling eggs against a boulder, using one's arms to stop a chariot, one weak and one strong, as different as sky and earth.

The full arsenal is in the hands of the bourgeoisie, that is certain. Because making or buying weapons (requires money), and one needs weapons to protect assets. The soldiers who shoot guns and fire cannons are merely seeking the bare minimum to live on, sacrificing themselves for others.

War can also be said to be the (robbery behavior) of a country. Behind the god of war stands a god of wealth | the economy, and the former must obediently follow the command of the latter. The economic conflicts between modern countries are becoming increasingly acute, quickly turning from economic war into gun and cannon war. In other words: modern warfare is about occupying colonies and seizing markets to absorb raw materials and sell finished goods, that's all there is to it. (Of course, this refers to direct wars between imperialist powers. The cases of weak countries accepting the instigation of imperialist powers and engaging in internecine warfare, such as the recent situation in Cuba... are another matter.)

Therefore, war creates opportunities for capitalists who manufacture or sell weapons, or other industrial magnates, to make a fortune: the laboring classes only suffer unemployment, displacement, and death... which can be regarded as a blessing from war, whether it is a victorious country or a defeated country. This is well demonstrated in the European War.

Speaking of the essence of war, it is indeed terrible and extremely cruel. (Wars lead to endless disasters), (war is dangerous and fraught with peril), whether in ancient or modern times, at home or abroad, everyone deeply detests and opposes it. Only a few with ulterior motives advocate war. But it's useless: oppose as you may, war is still war. And as science develops, war machines become more sophisticated, killing more people and causing greater destruction, by hundreds of millions times more than in the past. What is the reason for this? According to Sun Yat-sen, the total world population is 1.5 billion, of which 1.25 billion are oppressed, and only 250 million are oppressors. The oppressors, of course, are the armed class | the military and police are employed and directed by them: the oppressed on the opposite side have no assets and are naturally the unarmed class. It is as clear as day that three-quarters of the unarmed class will fail when opposing one-quarter of the armed class; however, if (thought is power) is true, then the psychology of so many people attacking the psychology of so few will inevitably lead to ultimate victory; and it seems that this opportunity may be in the near future.

If we want to be people of the present era and possess some common sense, then everyone should stand on the side of (anti-war); however, we must not blindly follow the crowd with muddled thinking. Although war is bad, we must also distinguish its nature: for example, the American war for independence from Britain, the war to liberate black slaves that led to the American Civil War, and the revolutions of the Paris Commune in France and the October Revolution in the Soviet Union, all had great value in human history, and we painfully express our sympathy.

Therefore, our position is: in the negative aspect, we oppose the war preparations of all countries, we oppose wars waged for the benefit of a few bourgeoisies, and we oppose the cycle of violence begetting violence; in the positive aspect, we support everyone preparing for war, and we support the 1.25 billion oppressed people of the world uniting and preparing for war against the 250 million oppressors.

Calligraphy and Painting of Modern Celebrities 328

Painting by Mr. Tong Xiaohe (Brief Biography)

Tong Chuanlin, courtesy name Yunong, sobriquet Xiaoqiu, also known as Lianxi Waishi, is a native of Jiading, Jiangsu Province. He was fond of the six principles of painting from a young age, and even more so in his later years. He learned from the Lou Dong school and modeled himself on the four masters of the Yuan dynasty, combining elegance and composure. His artistic attainments are between Peng Xin and Jiao Qi.

One Day Tian Yi Ping 329

This day was like any other peaceful day. There was no hurricane, no heavy rain. The working class had risen to work, and the bourgeois were searching for sweet dreams in their quilts. The sun poked its head from the east, shining into Mrs. Wang's bedroom. Her drowsy sleeping state was no longer visible on the bed, and Mr. Wang was already holding a newspaper and flipping through local news. Clearly, this day was different from peaceful days; at least something had happened at the Wang mansion to awaken this young couple from their sweet dreams.

At the same time, there were also chaotic sounds in the kitchen. Mrs. Wang was running up and down the stairs in her nightgown like a shuttle, she had to take care of everything when Mr. Wang got up, she had to order things in the kitchen. The entire Wang mansion was in a mess, only the two dark doors were tightly closed and did not move. After Mr. Wang finished reading the newspaper, he was urged diligently by Mrs. Wang, stretched out his arms, sat up, and a cigarette was sent to his lips. He took a puff of smoke and said like an ignorant child: "Is this little thing worth being so busy about?"

"It's your birthday, and you're lying in bed not getting up. Am I busy for the wrong reason?" Mrs. Wang's apple-like face, no matter how angry she was, burst out laughing after a while.

So we know that today is Mr. Wang's birthday.

In the hall hung a painting of a hundred longevity characters, a pair of golden characters written on red candles, inserted on the snow-white Three Principles flag, was so majestic, the steaming sacrificial offering attracted a little beggar who refused to leave outside the door.

Mr. Wang's relatives, friends, Mrs. Wang's relatives, friends, one by one dressed very beautifully as if attending a fashion exhibition. Our Mrs. Wang was no longer dressed as when she was shuttling back and forth, but had changed into a newly tailored georgette cheongsam. Her face was of course always smiling, welcoming every guest, handing out cigarettes, taking out melon seeds, and entertaining many guests, so naturally and so elegantly. Praises and congratulations. We know that today is Mr. Wang's twenty-eighth birthday.

The lively situation in the Wang mansion today changed from a lunch for the couple to five tables of wine and dishes. Male and female servants carried dishes back and forth, the host diligently urged them to drink, and the guests naturally drank heartily.

Today afternoon, it was also unlike the usual when the couple rushed to the cinema, leaving the servants to doze off. Upstairs and downstairs, three tables of mahjong were being played with a bang, and many people surrounded them as spectators. Everyone playing mahjong cracked melon seeds, puffed on cigarettes, and chatted with the people behind them, talking about how they had won a lot of money by calling a three-fan hand the day before, or how a big hand had been played wrong and was called by the opponent, but they were always paying attention to every card played. White board pong, fourteen, twenty-eight, twenty-four, forty-eight. The people who called laughed, and the people who didn't call also laughed, and the onlookers were of course happy, because today is Mr. Wang's twenty-eighth big birthday.

Mr. Wang, along with several friends who liked opium, huddled in the pavilion room, lying on the bed, sitting on the platform, burning black smoke, talking about the seventh and eighth ladies of Fuzhili and Yihongyuan. Whenever they talked about women, their eyebrows danced with joy. The laughter inside echoed the sound of cards outside. Today's special situation made the patrol officer in the lane also ask the amah who came back from fetching water in confusion: "What happy event is there at your master's house?"

"It's our young master's birthday." The amah replied with a smile, unlike the usual cursing "a thousand cuts".

Eating longevity noodles was another flurry of activity.

Dinner was especially a few hours later than usual, originally Mrs. Wang noticed that the wristwatch on her wrist was already ten o'clock and thought of starting dinner. The people playing mahjong, the onlookers, and the people in the pavilion room talking about women, time was not worth cherishing to them, let alone it being Mr. Wang's twenty-eighth small birthday.

Although the whole day had passed after the meal, it didn't hurt to borrow the time from tomorrow morning, and time didn't care about them anyway. This day was like any other peaceful day, there was no hurricane, no heavy rain, but the Wang mansion inside the two dark doors was experiencing an extraordinary day.

A young couple, after seeing off the guests, felt a slight weariness and went to bed when the sky was about to dawn.

The next day came as usual, the sun poked its head from the east and shone into Mrs. Wang's bedroom, here was quietly sleeping one person, everything was still like any other peaceful day.

(Disaster Relief Fundraising) Heart 330

The dusk after the autumn rain is a strangely interesting time: the playground is muddy and wet, and the leaves still drip with tiny drops of water; dense dark clouds and piled-up white mist are driven away by the newly blooming, delicate sunset, leaving them no place to stand. Low pressure turns into high pressure. People all feel relaxed, comfortable, and at ease. So, a few of us took chairs to the playground to enjoy this comforting time.

Suddenly, a group of yellow-faced young men in short clothes ran in, holding pens and inkstones and something that looked like yellow paper bound into a booklet. The words "Disaster Relief Fundraising" were crookedly written on the thin surface. Speaking Shanghai dialect with a northern accent, they spoke vividly like the painted faces on the opera stage:

"Gentlemen: We are here today to solicit some disaster relief donations from your school. You gentlemen must know about the great flood in the Hankou area in the past, where the water rose to several feet, harming the people and their homes. Recently, the Yellow River has breached its banks, and the people there are certainly suffering from disasters again. They are all our compatriots, and everyone should help each other. So,

Page 23

We have taken some free time to voluntarily come out to raise some donations to help them. We beg you gentlemen to give generously."

"Ah! You are enthusiastic philanthropists, coming to raise funds for the poor disaster victims, this is a most meritorious and reasonable thing, but we ourselves are also waiting for donations and relief from others!" We just perfunctorily brushed them off, with an attitude that was half-joking.

"Yes, gentlemen, since September 18th and January 28th, markets everywhere have declined, and the education sector has of course been similarly affected! We are well aware of this. However, we think of those who are suffering in the disaster now, living in a subhuman hell! We really can't bear to watch them suffer alive, and it is because of this sense of compassion that everyone should have, that we come here, not afraid of running around, to do this thing. Please gentlemen, don't just say polite words, we are all our own people, and it is right to help each other. We are always more fortunate than them, the water has not yet risen from under our feet: there is still food in our bellies, so we beg you gentlemen to give generously and donate as much as you wish, this is something that will accumulate infinite merit for you and your descendants!" The annoying fellows chattered on endlessly.

"In that case, I think it's better if we do this! We can't get much from the money of just a few of us, tomorrow I will solicit donations from our friends and the parents of the students of this school on your behalf, please leave an address, and I will write to you later to notify you to come and collect it!" Old Zhang cleverly seized their weakness.

Their faces changed, a forced bitter smile appeared on their faces, seemingly expressing that their trick could not succeed. "We poor people have no address," they muttered to themselves as they prepared to leave.

I listened quietly from the side, and finally, seeing their strange attitude, I felt a great deal of emotion! "The Yellow River breaching its banks" is an established fact, and "the disaster victims suffering a subhuman hellish life" is also just as much of an established fact like iron! Why did the Yellow River breach its banks? Should the disaster victims be given relief? Why are there actually people today who are using the guise of "disaster relief fundraising", with words sweeter than honey on their lips and the hearts of a bodhisattva, while in reality carrying out the deeds of wolves and dogs, collecting money under false pretenses? ... Whose responsibility is this? The Yellow River has breached its banks, and this society will also mature, with the same fate as the "Yellow River" drastically evolving! Who can still gloss over or deny this?

Autumn 331

The desolate autumn wind brings to the courtyard the sycamore trees with their fallen leaves, standing like bald men. The insects chirping in the fields add a touch of desolation.

On the radio, a shrill girl finished singing "Thank You, Drizzling Rain," and that familiar voice reported the news of the Chestnut King.

At the Rising Sun Building, where pedestrians throng, the giant chimney belches smoke. Two strong arms hold an iron shovel that could kill a person with one blow, slaughtering the gifts of autumn in the scorching black sand. Each bag contains twelve, the fragrant, sweet Liangxiang chestnuts. A crowd of people surrounds, chewing and savoring the shrill girl singing "Thank You, Drizzling Rain" that emanates from the radio.

Peeling chestnuts and walking along Nanjing Road, among the many "big sale" banners, you can once again feel that autumn has come. The Mooncake Fair, do you know? The Mid-Autumn Festival, when you raise your head to gaze at the bright moon and bow your head to think of your hometown, is just around the corner. At the Mooncake Fair, a model of Emperor Tang Minghuang touring the Moon Palace moves his hand inside the glass window illuminated by neon lights. There is no need for me to deliberately point out that, like at the chestnut stall, a crowd surrounds, I don't know if they are paying attention to the Emperor Tang Minghuang touring the Moon Palace toy, or salivating over that tower-like big mooncake?

Shanghai changes with the four seasons, but the people living in the Shanghai environment don't feel it! For example, with the Chestnut King and the Mooncake Fair, Shanghai people only know that these are two seasonal products of the present, they don't know that the desolate autumn and the heavily snowy winter are closely following behind.

Because if we turn a corner, it's the silk street that has a big sale all year round. The pitiful music of Autumn Fragrance is sent over day in and day out, a nonstop big sale... shameless advertising. This is also a seasonal product of the present, not for the sake of the children wearing new clothes; at this time, they dare to come up with this kind of plaything. Among the customers who crowd inside, there are many who have clothes they have never worn hidden at the bottom of their boxes.

Now I should talk about the women of autumn. The women of autumn are no different from the women of summer, thin clothes, bare legs, but they no longer have the courage to go to the swimming pool. Of course, women also know that it is cooler now than in the past, but for the future, they need to start training early to avoid digging a well when they are already thirsty and buying a plaster for a sore only when it hurts. Men are not so energetic, you see thick gray flannel suits already hanging on their bodies, like advertising mannequins in shop windows, and those artistic students with dirty feet have also moved their only evergreen serge suits onto their bodies, and if you compare them to your sweetheart hanging on your arm, you should really be ashamed!

"It's September 18th again!" someone said.

I heard a conversation about autumn next to the tram stop.

"What September 18th?" someone said.

"Today is September 18th!"

"Oh. I thought I bought 126918."

Why don't I ever run into 226622? Sometimes I think that too. The second issue is like the current toy, one yuan per strip, you have to give up smoking for a month to buy this strip. The amazing number of 50,000 yuan often wakes me up from my dreams; but so far I can't spare a yuan to touch my forehead |

However, I hope that this issue's special prize for that dear brother of my dreams is precisely 126918, a newly made camel hair robe, or waiting for him at his maternal uncle's house!

Drama

War and Peace (2) (9) (A Play in Four Acts) by Ling He 332

Act Three: A Eulogy to Peace

Voice: (Is madam inside?) Must I say it again? You've made such a mess of me.

Military Authority: It's all your fault; who told you to give me that kind of book to read?

Wife: (Laughing, coming from inside, leaning on her husband) That book is truly amusing. (Sits down) Ah, I'm so exhausted. I think we should go in and lie down for a while.

Military Authority: You go and sleep; I'll rest here for a moment... Why hasn't Secretary He returned yet?

Wife: Where did you send him?

Military Authority: I told him to go to Tian Yuping to inquire about his opinion on the government's telegram.

Wife: That Tian Yuping? The one who was sent last week to preside over political affairs?

Military Authority: That's right.

Wife: What? Didn't you say he was making things difficult for you everywhere? Why do you want to go to him to inquire about anything?

Military Authority: He's making things difficult for me? Humph! But this time, the credit for negotiating peace should be given to him anyway.

Wife: No matter what you do, I want to ask you: What do you plan to do? I've told you hundreds of times that, no matter what, I want you to send me back to Shanghai. Several planes came a few days ago and already frightened my mother. It has tired her old self so much she sent a telegram to ask. If the Japanese soldiers really disregard faith and start attacking Qiping without any reason, don't scare me to death.

Military Authority: Look! You're being childish again. Can't you rest assured? How could I bear to let you be frightened with me?

Wife: Then why aren't we leaving? Why do we have to live here in suspense?

Military Authority: Why do you have to live in suspense? Didn't I say you can rest assured?

Wife: Are you sure the peace talks will succeed?

Military Authority: Why wouldn't they succeed? As long as we are sincere on our side.

Wife: That's true, but if the conditions are bad, our money in the Bank of Taiwan will be in trouble.

Military Authority: Yes, for our own sake, we must cease hostilities.

Young Master: (Entering from the right side door, crying) Waaah... I'm going to tell Daddy... Waaah... (Goes upstairs)

Orderly: Good young master, good young master (Following behind him), please forgive me. Come on, shall I take you riding a horse?

Young Master: No, who wants to ride a horse? I'm going to tell.

Military Authority: (Hearing the crying) You bastard, who is bullying the child again? (Goes into the inner room immediately. Appears on the stairs shortly after.) What is it again? (Wife also follows behind)

Young Master: Daddy! This bastard cheated my money.

Military Authority: What?

Orderly: That's not true, sir.

Young Master: He wanted me to play poker with him.

Military Authority: (Raises his hand and slaps the orderly's cheek) Why did you teach him to gamble? You have some nerve!

Young Master: He took my money. I had four Aces, and he also had four Aces, but he insisted that the heart one was bigger. Daddy, I forgot what you taught me last time. You said, is the spade bigger or the heart bigger?

Military Authority: Are you a spade or a heart?

Young Master: I'm a spade.

Military Authority: Then of course the spade is bigger.

... Don't laugh. Remember in the future, the spade is bigger. (Orderly retreats) Don't cry. Let's play hide-and-seek. Auntie will play too. It will be so fun.

Young Master: Okay, I'll be it, you guys hide.

(The Military Authority covers his son's eyes, and crawls under the table himself. The auntie also hides. Afterward, the son comes to find them, and the Military Authority crawls back and forth on the ground. Before long, the Confidential Secretary pushes open the door on the right side and enters, laughing when he sees the scene. The Military Authority feels embarrassed and quickly stands up.)
